 **(10)** **करगरा इति अभिधानं यस्याः — करगराभिधाना **— by name, karagara **(करे गरं यस्याः सा**–with poison in her hand) **यथार्थ नाम यस्याः सा–यथार्थनाम्नी**–with a significant name. **सर्वजन्तूद्वेगकारिणी **— troubling all the people. **द्वारदेशत्रुक्षस्थितः **— sitting on the tree, standing near her door. **अन्य–देशः – देशान्तरं–तस्य अभिमुखंः — देशान्तराभिमुखः अभूत्**–went to another Country. **मम अतिथिना**

**भाव्यम् **– be my guest **यथावत् उपकर्तव्यम् एव **– I must oblige you accordingly. **मदनभूपतिसनाथाम् **– ruled by **मदनपति**. **नीरुजा**–free from disease. **मान्त्रिक **– Those who can remove diseases with the help of **मन्त्र. मन्त्रवादः न एव विधेयः **– you need not say any mantras. **व्यन्तरेण आविष्टा **– haunted by a ghost. **समुचितं पुरस्कारं **– due reward. **घोषेण दत्ता **– proclaimed, **डिण्डिमः स्पृष्टः **–Touched the drum to show that he accepted the proclamation. **आचार्य विस्तरम् **– all the paraphernelia of a **आचार्य** to show that he was a learned man.

** ( 11 )** **अत्रान्तरे **– In the meanwhile. **पितृष्वसा **– aunt. **जीवितशेषा. (जीवितमेव शेषः यस्याः सा)**–lit. with her bare life. She barely mannaged to live. **मया प्रतिपन्नम् एकदेशे कृतम् **– I have done what I promised in one case viz. the **राजकन्या** was left by him. **मन्त्र** and **तन्त्रम् – मन्त्र** is chanting while **तन्त्र** is doing all the necessary operations. **कृतः अञ्जलिः येन **– folding his hands (generallyin reverence ) **तत् व्याख्यातुम् **–To tell that viz that **करगरा** was come.

** (12) पात्रम् **– Viz that **सुलोचना. पुत्तलिका**–A golden circular piece used in ornaments (cf.**पुतळी **in marathi.) **घृतौदनं–घृतं च ओदनं च तयोः समाहारः **– Ghee and rice. **स्वेच्छावृत्ति **–The life of a vagabond or libertine. **जन्मशतं नानायोनीः प्राप्नोति **– It has to go through a number of stages (viz. lives of many animals) According to Hindu philosophy (**आत्मा** is quite distinent **शरीर** from or body which is merely its cloak and it remains in & **शरीर** only Temporarily . **महान् सन्तापः भविष्यति **–You shall have to suffer very heavily. **बालभाव **– Child hood. **यौवनेन तुष्टं चित्तं येषां ते – यौवनतुष्टचित्ताः** Proud of their youth. **शिशिरे अपवस्त्राः **– Like men without clothes in cold season. **किं **– what is the use of **देहिन्देहः विद्यते यस्य **– lit one who has a body i. e. man, **अकुलीनः **– not born in a high family **तैः **– In sanskrit, plural is used when Speaking about a great man. **सिद्धसारस्वतमन्त्र – मन्त्र**–are said to be **सिद्ध** in the hands of man when he can use them efficiently.

** (13) अनुचित्या **– A thing to be pondered over. **संसारासारता **– the futulity of this life. **चलितवृत्तम् **– a man of unsteady character. **कस्मात् उद्विजितव्यम् **– from what should we turn away. **संसारः एव अरण्यम् – संसाराण्यं तस्मात् **– from the forest (i. e. entanglement) of this world **दृष्टादृष्टार्थलाभाय **— For the attainment of present and furure ends. **न्याय्य न्यायात् अनपेतं न्याय्यम् **— In the just path. **विद्युत् विलसितम् **—flash of lightening (It is very transient.) **कुलशीलनिष्प्रपञ्चा **— Men who do not look to the **कुल** or **शील** of other. **चिन्तामणिः **– A rare jewel, supposed to give us what we want. **प्रविगतं तमः येभ्यः – प्रविगततमसः**–enlightened. **त्यागसमेतम् **– Coupled with charity. **कुलमेव कमलं, तस्य दिनेशः कुलकमलदिनेशः** The sun of the lotus of his family i. e. a shining star of the family. **परधनहृदयहरा – परेषां धनं च हृदयं च हरतीति **–Captivating the heart and wealth of others. **विवेकवत्ता **– power of discrimination. **दान्तः**–One who has control overoncself. **कमला **– goddess of wealth. **नीतिवृत्त **–A man of good moral conduct. **सालस्यः **– Idle man. **धीरविभवेन**–with steady wealth. **पिशुनयुत् **– Malicious **प्रणतकलत्रेण **— one with an obedient wife **(प्रणतङ्कलत्रंयस्य ) स्वभ्यस्ता **–wellacquired. **(सु + अभ्यस्ता). मुक्ता भरणा**–pearl ornament **(आभरणम् )**.

** ( 14 )** **प्रातः अस्मरणीयेत्त्वात् **– Not fit to be thought of in the morning time. The morning time is very holy and hence one is expected to think of good things and not of such men as misers. **कलान्तरवाणिज्यादिभिः वर्तुलीकृतवित्तः **– Amassed a large for tune in trade and industries. **दुर्भिक्ष **— Famine. **एकाकी पुरुषः श्रीमान् **– A man is rich only when alone i.e when his family expenses are not upon him. **अन्येन सुहृदः सर्वे **– All others are friends (in name only). **धनमूलं कुटुम्बकम् **– Family has its basis in riches i.e. one can have, Family only when one has money where with to support them. **अनागतांवक्षां करोमि **– I shall make a provisiou **(अवेक्षा)** for the future **(अनागत)**. **परालक्ष्यस्थाने–परै अलक्ष्ये स्थाने **– Itn a place not seen by others i. e. in a secret place. **परिवार**–Dependants. **कण्ठगतप्राण **– About to die. Construe: - **तत् (धनं) प्रार्थयद्भिः मम प्राणाः किन्नैव गह्यन्ते यतः धने (मम) शुचः न स्युः **–Wealth is the very life of a miser; and when you ask me for it, you can as well take my life so that I need not mourn for the (loss of) it. **प्राणमात्रावशेषः **— Barely keeping alive. **निराकुलः **—Comfortably, without any pangs (of conscience). **निजप्राणान् नश्यतः अनुमन्यसे **– How do you allow yourself to be starved (lit killed) when you have got money. **दानभोगभवं सुखम् **— Pleasure arising from charity or enjoyment of wealth. **भुज्यते यत् न कामतः **— Which is not enjoyed with pleasure. **किमपि कुरुत**– do as you like, say what you will. **प्राणव्ययेनापि–स्वी क्रियते**– I would not prefer the loss of life even to loss of wealth. **घनपोटलकम् **– small bundle containing money. **नाविकं धीवरम् **–fisherman. with a boat. **त्यक्तकामेन **–Though I have no desire, to sav my life. **परिवारशोकाकुलम् **– Grieved at the loss of family. **वेतनत्वेन **– By way of the hire of your services (for killing the miser). **दित्सा **– Desiderative of **दा**–desire to give **दाहविशुद्धानि **– purified by burning i. e. melting. **पुण्यार्थम् एव **–for charity's sake. **कृतार्थः **– one who has attained his end; hence happly or successful. **जनयति**–The subject is the wealth of a miser. **मङ्गल न प्रसूते **– Does not give rise to any good Act. **परिहरति यशांसि **– Deprives a man of his fame. **ग्लानिम् आविष्करोति **– Produces exhaustion. **उपकृति रहितानां** and **सर्वभोगन्युतानां** qualify. **सम्पदां **– miser's wealth does not help anybody nor does it give any enjoyment to him. **दुर्विपाकः **– A fatal result; an evil end.

** ( 15 ) सत्वानि **— animals. **एकैकसत्वपरिकल्पनव्यवस्था **— an arrangement by which one animal was to be given daily. **शशक **– rabbit. **वारक **–Turn. **कराल **– fierce. **वेलातिक्रमः **– delay. **झम्पाम् अदात् **– Jumped. **अल्पसत्वेन**–of fecble strength. **इषुः **– arrow. **सराष्टं–राष्ट्रेन संहित **– with the nation to help him. **मन्त्रिनिश्चयः **—The will of a minister.

** (16 ) सचिवाग्रणीः **– Prime-minister. **बुद्धिविभवाक्रान्तः **– Overcome by the power of his genius. **करदा **— Paying trilute or taxes. **सानुरागेण (अनुरागेण सहित) **– Devoted, attached. **कः गुणः स्यात् **– What is the use of Possessing intellect and bravery Construe: – **येषां प्रज्ञाविक्रमभक्तयः गुणाः नृपते भूतये समुदिताः ते भृत्या, इतरे सम्पत्सु, आपत्सुच नृपतेः कलत्रम्**—Those alone, are the real servants of a king who exert their, brains, bravery and devotion for the benefit of their king; others are merely his wives through adversity and prosperity. **प्रज्ञागुप्तशरीरस्य प्रज्ञया गुप्तंशरीरं यस्य सः **– whose body is protected by his genius. **संहताः **– United. qualifies **अरयः हस्तोपधृछत्रः **–one with umbrella in his hands. **निर्द्रव्याञ्च मेदिनीं विदधानः **–making the earth poor. **अवटः **– pit. **घोटिका द्वयम् **–a pair of horses. **शालिहोत्र **– an expert in horses. sloka 3. the poet contrasts the loss of a servant with the loss of a country. **दण्डपाशिकम् **– the **कोतवाल **–a police officer. **पूर्वोद्दिष्टं भक्तम् **– when tbrown into the pit the king had ordered certain rations to be given to him; the kotwal means to say, someone rceives them but he could not say who individually. **स्वामी दुर्णय** etc.– a Teacher in warding off form evil things. **विश्रम्भे हृदयम् **– A heart to confide things i.e. very confidential, just tike one's heart. **नियोग **– orders. **सप्तसमुद्र** etc. **रशना एव दाम रशनादाम** (**रशना **— girdle round the waist **दामन् **– rope). **सप्तसमुद्राणां सीमा एव रशना दाम तत्** a which is bounded by the girdle of 7 oceans **सर्वकारम् अभूः **— You have served me in all these relations. **को वा न कर्णो मम **—this is attributed to **दुर्योधन.** He means to says that was all in all to him: “whatis not Karna to me in i. e. Karna serves me in all capacities. Similarly here the king was served by his minister **सपर्याणम् (पर्याणेन) **— harnessed. **बाह्यालि **— outer lane.

** (17) मखमुख्ये **– the principal man at the or sacrifice. **मितभवत्** etc.– **मितम् भवता अर्पितम वसनं, अशनञ्च तेनैव जीवनं येषां ते **— who are living on the scanty food and clothing which you have given them. The poet means to say he can not depend upon such people. The style and reasoning of these Aryas correspond to **मोरोपन्त**’s **संशयरत्नमाला.** They are of & devotional **सर्वदे त्वयि** etc.–How can this ignorance befit you when you are ominscient. **लिप्सा**—desiderative from **लभ्** to get. **दातरिदित्सा** etc.—but the desire to give is quite thrown away by the donor even though the mendicant is wishing it. This is called **कृपण**. **कथा**–a bad conduct. **रङ्कम् **— a lowly man. **स्वात्मना एवा मे वृत्तिं कुरु**—Maintain me by yourself. **सामान्यम् इव विशेषः **– like an excaption to a rule **(सामान्यम्)**. The poet means to say, that as a general rule, he is kind to all; and why is he an exception in his case. **मानुषी **— woman. **लोलद्भुजपदमस्तक **— With the head, hands and feet drooping; i. e. in a very miserable condition. **ते विरुदमाला न रथैः उपयाति **– the garland of your praises can not be carried away even when loaded in chariots; i. e. Rama’s virtues and the praise for the same is so great in extent that even chariots can not carry it. In other words, his virtues are innumerable. **विष्टपगीतम् **— a song sung by all. **पल्वल इव** etc. — just as the cloud supplies water to a small pool without receiving any service from him; so you give me help though I have not served you. **सेवक वंश भवत्वात्**—being born from a family which had served you. **निजजाठरवह्नेः जयाय**—lit. for the appeasing of the fire in the stomach i. e. for the sake of their bread. **अज्ञालसंसतीतसन्ततपीडा परम्पराशात्यै **—f or preventing harm to one's ignorant and indolent posterity. **चित्तचमत्कृतकारणम् **– strange. **त्वन्मुख सौरभचर्वित ताम्बूलाशम् **— expecting to get the fragrant ताम्बूल Imasticated in your mouth. **सन्मुखतायै चिबुकं** (chin ) **करेण कर्षन्तम् **— touching his mother's chin with his hand so that she may turn her face towards him. **सिन्दूराचलवासिनि **— residing on the **सिन्दूर** mountain **(अचल)**. **रामाभिधे** qualifies **मातूः (राम इति अभिधा यस्याः सा.)**

** (18)** **संसर्गबर्बर**–A blockhead by company i. e. one who becomes a blockhead by keeping bad company. **हीनसंसर्ग**—company with low born. **बालिशः **- ignorant; fool; purile. **प्रचरतृणाङ्कुरा **— rich in grass. **स्थली **— Lit. place; here pasture ground. **गोरक्षणोपजीविनः **— living on cow-tending. **अदुष्टपुरुषव्यवहार **— who had not seen much of life. **जरती **— old. **त्वदेकगतिः**—wholly depending upon you. **पोषण साध्यं हि** etc.—old men can pull on if properly cared by others. **मातृस्नेहपरवशः **– overcome by the love for his mother. **गोपोषणपदार्थव्युत्पन्न **— expert in cattle-feeding, **परिपाटि**–Method, Routine of the मराठी–परिपाठः. गोपुच्छलोम (hair) चित्रित दाम्ना (rope) with a rope variegated with hairs from cows’ tails. **गले बद्ध्वा **–Tieing her by neck. **करीषाग्निम् **– fire produced by burning dry cow-dung. **घासकवलप्रदान **— offering her morsels of grass. **वराकी **– A poor woman. **तथा पराभवम् अनुभवन्ति **— Insulted in this manner. **प्रतिवेशिगोपैः **— neighbourly cowherds. **जीवनादृष्ट जीवितः **– who had seen nothing of life save that required for his livelihood.

** (19)** **गणकः **— Astrologer. **पुत्रमनोरथेन **– with the affection of a son i. e. very affectionately. **पदार्थं न अधिगच्छति **— does not know the meaning of any word. **परितोषवान् **— willingly. **लोकद्वयं प्रत्याशायाः अङ्कुरः **— His son was the source of his hopes i. e. basis of happiness both in this and the next world. **सकलमनोरथस्थानम् **–Note the use of this in neuter gender. See note

1st lesson the centre of all his aspirations. **कर्मातरपाम्मुखः **— Disregarding his other pursuits. **तस्य इच्छया अवहितः **— According to the bend of his mind. **महता समयेन **—after a good deal of time. **राज्ञः परिचितगुणं करोमि **— I shall bring his merits to the notice of the king. **प्रश्नं जानाति **— knows how to read the future. **अङ्गुलीयक **— ring. **मुष्टौकृत्वा **— holding in his palm **कण्ठिनीम् आदाय **— taking a chalk stick. **शास्त्रानुसारेण **— according to scientific rules **संवादिनी वाक् **— A consistent speech. **मण्डलाकृति **– Circular. **गुरुद्रव्यं** &c. the thing is costly and is hollow in the middle. **जातरभसः**—becoming impatient. **पुलकितबाहमूलः – पुलकाः सञ्जाताः यस्मिन् तत् - पुलकितं बाहुरमूलंयस्य **— with his hairs standing on the arms (in joy). **निजोहेन**—**ऊह**—-gueos or conjecture. **पाषाणघट्टकमण्डलम्**—a round grinding stone. **शास्त्रानुसारिण्यागणनया**—Scientific calculation. **तावत् संवादः एव**–There was consistency. **अव्याप्तिमूलकः तर्कः**—According to Sanskrit logicians, a definition is wrong either when it is **अतिव्याप्त**–It is **अव्याप्त** when the definition does not include what it ought to include and **अतिव्याप्त** when it includes what it ought not to include. Thus the definition of a Brahmin as is liable to both these objections. because it does not include a **सन्न्यासी** who has not got **शिखा** or **सूत्र**; and it includes many though they are non-Brahmins, **तर्क** is the science of logic; a conclusion wanting in invariable concomitance (i. e. which is the thing necessary for a proper definition) i. e. it should be niether **अव्याप्त** nor **अतिव्याप्त तर्क** a here means conclusion. In the following statement we have neither **अतिव्याप्ति** nor **अव्याप्ति** c.f **यत्र** **यत्र धूमः तत्र तत्र वह्निः** and hence there is invariable concomitance. **यावत् अम्बुधि**—the sea marked the termination of Travels; Travel by sea being then quite uncommon.

 **(20) तैलङ्गाभिजनः**—an inhabitant of Telangana **महीसुरसत्तमः**—best of the Bramhins **वेदान्तशास्त्र, न्यायवेदान्तदर्शन, पूर्वमीमांसा, महान्भाष्य**—are some of the important branches of study for a Pandit **आश्रयेच्छया**—with a desire to get some support. **शक्रोपमवैभवस्य**—having wealth vying with that of Indra. **मध्यमे वयसि**—middle of life.

 **(21) जनपदः**—country. **सभासीनस्य (सभायाम् आसीनस्य)**—while sitting in his council. **आसन्नचरस्य कोशाधिकारिणः**—The treasurer who was near at hand. **क्रीडामर्कटपोताय**—a young one of a monkey kept for sport. **रक्षिणां हस्तच्युताय**—having escaped from the hands of its keepers. **भाण्डागारिक**–Treasurer **रस्मिज्वालाकुलान्**—lustrous. **विजनं नीत्वा**—Taking him aside. **साचिव्यसापेक्षं साधननम्**—An act requiring help. **श्रमणः**—A Sanyasi. **कृष्णचतुर्दश्याम्**—14th day of the dark half. **बाढम्**—surely, certainly. **क्षान्तिशीलः **— **क्षान्तिः शीलं यस्य सः**—Patient.

 **(22)** **नीलवसनेन समलङ्कृतशिराः **— Tying a blue cloth round his head. **दक्षिणामुखं गत्वा**—going in a Southernly direction. **सत्यसङ्गरः **— **सत्यः सङ्गरः यस्य**—whose promise was true i. e. faithful **छिन्नरज्जूम् **— after cutting the rope that tied him to the tree. **अट्टहासम् अकरोत् **— laughed loudly. **वेतालाधिष्टितम् **— haunted by a ghost. **वज्रादपि अखण्डितम् अकम्पच**—harder and firmer than even adamant. **अध्वविनोदाय **—to pass our time on the way.

** (23)** **सतां वर्त्म **— the paths of the virtuous **मार्गर्स्थः न अवसीदति **— one who tries ( to go along their paths) will not fail completely. **तेन अश्मानः अपि देवताः **— owing to these qualities, even stones become gods. **जपतः न अस्ति पातकम् **— one would not commit sins when one is reciting (holy things). **सुलभा सा अन्यजन्मनि **— Refers to the doctrine of rebirth; whatever we have tried to do in this life will be done far more easily by us in the next life; we carry with us all the desires and ambitions of this life. Therefore, if we can not succeed in this life, we can easily do so in the next, **परेषाम् अपवादः एव सस्यम्**–**परवादसस्यम् **– the poet compares our conduct to a cow and the censures of the public about us to grass. The cow (our conduct) should not be allowed to stray upon the grass (i. e. scandals). **अनागतविधातारम् **–who provides **(विधाता)** for the future **(अनागत) स्थिरारम्भम् **– steady **श्रीः वरम् उपतिष्ठते **–the goddess of wealth marries only such a bridgeroom.

** (24)** **तदायतिः **— from that time. **अत्यादृतः **— expert.** दण्डनीति **— **राजनीति**—politics **प्रगल्मवाच् **— a lengthy speech. **अर्थशास्त्रेषु आत्मसंस्कारम् अप्रतिपद्य **— not having got initiation into political science. **अनग्निशोधिता **– not melted in fire. **अत्युच्छ्रितः **–exalted. **परैः अध्यारुह्यमाणम् **— influenced by others. **साध्यं **— end and **साधन **–means. **सर्वाः स्थितीः सङ्किरेयुः **— will throw affairs into confusion. **इतः अमुतः च लोकात्**—from this and the next world. **आगमः एव दीपः** **। तेन दृष्टः आगमदीपदृष्टः **— lighted by the lamp of knowledge. **दिव्यं चक्षुः** etc. is in apposition with **शास्त्रन्नाम् **— verily science is celestial vision into etc. **व्यवहित **– hidden concealed **विप्रकृष्ट **– Distant, remote. **अप्रतिहतवृत्ति — **meets with no difficulty. **अर्थदर्शनेषु असामार्थ्यात् **— because of his inability to understand the situation of affairs **बाह्यविदया **— Such as **नृत्यगीत, काव्य** etc.

 **(25)** **आसमुद्रम् **— upto the seas. **उत्कर्षासहिष्णुः **— jealous of his prosperity. **तुरष्कैः**—the Turks. **निम्नाभिमुखं पततः पयसः** etc–waters falling down wards from higher level. **रिपुत्रासभग्नस्य **— scattered by the force of the enemy. **विपक्षं खड्गधारा प्रहारपरि कृतशिरस्कम् **— sever the head of your enemy with the stroke of our swords **पुलकालङ्कृत बाहुमूलः **– **पुलकाभिः** **अलकृतं बाहुमूलं यस्य सः **–with hairs standing on his arms (in joy). **कुलिशपाताधिकेन **— very severe. **कशाघातेन **— striking with a whip **(कशा)**. **अतर्कितः एव **— quite unexpectedly. **जितारिसैन्यम् – जितम् अरि सैन्यं येन सः** qualifies **काफरराम सितापपत्रपरिचितम् **— distinguishable by his white umbrella. **तुलितपार्थेन **— who can be compared with **पार्थ** i. e. as brave as Arjun.

 **(26)** **दितीयः अंश **— second part **बडुतरनाराच भिन्न शरीरे **— body, pierced with a number of arrows **(नाराच ). पुष्पितं किं शुक्रम् इव**–A Kinshuka tree in flowers looks very red; and therefore his body with blood gushing forth in all direc- tions is compared to it. **यस्य हितेच्छया**–with a view to whose benefit. **तेन विज्ञायमानः**–when appreciated by him. **श्रमपादपः** **फलितः **— lit. the tree of my labours has borne fruit i. e. my labours have been rewarded. **आपुङ्खनिमग्नात् **– stuck deep as far as the feathered part of the arrows **(पुङ्ख)**. **निर्वाणक्षतम् **– free from the wounds of the arrows. **सत्यपक्षानुरोधेन **— In accordance with his habit of telling the truth. **को वा अध्यगमिष्यत् **— who could have known. **परोच्छिष्टजीवी **– lit living upon the food, left by others after eating ; that is, living upon the glories won by others. **महेच्छः **— one with & noble mind. **विदग्धः **— accomplished.

** (27)** **मेधाविन् **— a man of genius. **धारणावती **— capable of retaining ( what is learnt ). **गौडविषये **–Territory of the **गोड. कविपण्डितः **– lerned poet. **नलचरिताभिधानम् - नलचरितम् इति अभिधानं यस्यतत्**–by name **नलचरित् परामृष्टवान् **– thought to himself **रसवत् **– possessing the Rasas e. g. **शृङ्गार, वीर** etc. **मानसग्राहिगुणालङ्कारसयुन्तम् **–possessing attractive merits and figures of speech. **अलङ्कार **– figures of speech e. g. **रुपक, उपमा** etc. **कवीनां** etc.–such a poem contributes to his fame; while others draw ridiculeus on him. **सद्भिः यत्न अनुगृह्यते **– which is not appreciated by the learned. **स्वर्णम् **— gold. **सदसि **– In the assembly of learned. **वारणसीम्** **उद्दिश्य जगाम **– went to Benares. **समाधौतिष्ठति **– was absorbed in profound contemplation **स्वदेशीय वात्सल्येन **— out of regard for his country man ( viz. **कोकपण्डित**) **बुद्ध्या –**Intentionally. **सदसत्विवेकप्रत्याशा **— with a hope that the good and had points ( in the poem ) may be pointed out. **कर्ण न अपर्यति **– does not lend his ear. **शब्दार्थयोः उहापोहेन सन्दर्भ** etc. – I shall pass my opinion after ascertaning the context and discussing the words and their sense (as used in your poem.) **मनसि निर्धारितम् **— I have fixed it in my mind **मासम् आकर्णितानि **— heard for one month **दोषान् समाधा **—reconciled the defects **विशेषान् उद्बोध्य **— pointed out many particularitics **हृष्टमनसं **—one with a light heart i. e. jolly or delighted.

 **वस्तुदोषम् अपहृत्य **– Regardless of the defects. **तद्विदः **– learned. **कण्टकिनः पुष्प**–flowers of a thory tree. **षट्पदाः **– bees.

** (28) उभयं त्वमेव मे**–you are both, father and mother to me. **जानकीजाने–जानकी जाया यस्य सः **— (whose wife was Janaki )— **गुरुकार्यम्**—Important buslness. **तव अश्लाघ्यम् **— This is improper on your part. Stauza 7 the poet means to say:- “People suspect me to be a hypocrite; because, I am not favoured by you; as hypocrites are not favoured by you. Just as a child whose tongue has been burnt by hot milk, tries to cool down even buttermilk before drinking it though there is no fear of buttermilk ever being hot. **सर्पिः** (Ghee) **पायसे एव भस्मनि किं नाम करोति**–Ghee when poured in milk is useful but what can it do when poured on Ashes; so the name Rama when uttered by others can produce good results, but with me a sinner, it is not effective. **वारि अपि भस्मीभवति** (**च्वी **form)–Even water disappears. Stanza 11 **माषः** is a black corn; we can not pick up anything out of a heap of such corn because of its blackness as the whole is black (**मालिन्यदोष**–the fault of being impure i. e. black) I. e. as everything is black so the picking of a few things would not make it all right. So the poet says, as his body is full of faults (lit sins), the chanting (of Rama’s name) can not separate the faults (as it would have done, if he had possessed only a few). In other words, being too sinful, even such chanting can not make him pure. **जल्पन्पक्षी**—A certain bird is supposed to peck at stones even though all the while, he is uttering to himself that the should not do such a foolish thing **(इत्थं साहसम् मा कुरु)**; so the poet, all the while speaking against sins, has been committing them. owing to his natural faults **(सहजैः दोषैः)**. **मृगमदभूमि **– Soil with musk due to the droppings of the musk deer. An onion **(पलाण्डुः)** even growing upon such a soil is not free from its bad odour. **(दोषम्)**. **परिगणना भगणानाम् भविता **— the number of stars can be counted **अणू**–smallest particles of matter.

** (29)** **किं वदन्ती **— rumour, report. **लब्धजनि **— born (lit, taken his birth ). **संस्कृतः **–initiated. **यथायथम् अकृताभ्यासः**–not. studying properly **यथेच्छाचारी **— vagabond **पोरोहितीं वृत्तिम् **— priestly duties. **महापण्डितप्ररोहक्षम **— ( a seat) fit to be used (for sitting) only by a great Pund it. **महतीं ग्लानिं प्राप्तुवन**—becoming very sorry. **कृतदेहत्यागनिश्चयतया **– with a will to sacrifice himself. **अनश्नत् **–not eating anything. **तस्याः कृपया कटाक्षाः । तत् एव अमृतम् । तेन स्त्रातः **– bathed in the nectar of her kindly looks i. e. favoured by her. **पण्डितप्रवर **— a great pundit. **महतीं प्रतिष्ठाम् अवाप **– rose to high distinction.

** (30)** **तुला**–balance. **वरं यानम्**—t is better to go **विषमे**–In difficulties, **तुलामात्रधनः **–with the balance only for his wealth i. e. having nothing except a balance. **प्रच्छन्नम् **–secretly. **दुःखपूरितातरङ्गः**—filled with grief **श्येन**–a hawk, falcon. **गजन्तत्र **etc.– In that case, a hawk can carry away even an elephant; and if it carries a child only, that should not cause susprise. **सकलम् उदन्त्तजातम्**–all that had happened from the beginning. **दण्डितः **— punished.

** (31)** **अमात्यप्रवरः **— an able miniter (just as **इन्द्र** had in **बृहस्पति**.) **निर्वासितः** (causal)—was expelled **कृष्णसार **— black autelope. **मार्गे लग्नः **— left behind. **भल्लूक, शार्दूल**—bear. **सहस्रवरदक्षिणाः **— In which more than thousand are given as **दक्षिणा**. **द्वीपिन्**—Tiger. **तरणिः** Sun. **आभूतसम्प्लवम्**—**सम्प्लव** is a the deluge which is supposed to occur at the end of this world when the whole earth is floodded with water **अप्रमत्तः**–awake.

** (32)** **तस्य प्रत्ययः ज्ञातः**–we now see the results of that bad omen. **अरुढः **— without a rider. **स्वस्थः **— free from disease **तन्निराससमये **– At the time of his expulsion. **भवितव्यतानुसारिणी **– following destiny. **सा** mears **तादृशी **– of that type; in accordance with our destiny, we have our desires, hopes etc. **करतलगतम् **– which is entirely in our hands. **घोषणा **– proclamation. **जवनिकान्तः स्थित **– sitting behind the curtain. **विदग्धता **– wisdom. **गङ्गासागरसङ्गामम् **– where the Ganges flows into the sea; regarded as very holy **(गङ्गायाः सागरस्य सङ्गमः यस्मिन् ।)** **मुच्यते **– freed from sins. **द्विजाति **– lit twicə born-i. e. Bramhins **क्षमापनयाचनम् **– begged his apology.

** (33)** **यावनालान् अवपत्**–sowed the Yavanala corn (**यावनाल** corresponds to millets). **प्रोन्नते भूप्रदेशे **– elevated or rising ground) so chosen forwarding off the birds attacking the corn.) **मञ्च **– an elevated shed in a field for a watch-man. **पस्तावः **–opportunity **अपथगामिनः **— wrongdoers. **ब्रह्मस्वम् **– wealth of a Bramhhin. **यावनालकदण्ड **— stalks of Yavanala plant. **उर्वारकम् **— fruits of cucumbers. **ब्राह्मणाभ्यर्थम् अनादृत्य **– out of respect to the Bramhin's request. **भुसुरः **— Bramhins (lit god on this earth.) **द्विजनिर्यापण **– scaring away the birds **(द्विज)** **आर्तिः **— Distress, sufferings. **केदारम् **– field. **धिषणा **— Intellect here; (creates such ideas in his mind). **जलतैलं विस्तारं याति **– oil spreads all over water when they are mixed. **मनाग् **– a little **खले गुहयम् **– a secret entrusted to a villain spreads i.e. he circulates it and does not keep it a secret. **त्वया अविदितम् **&c. you knew everything. **सुरपादयः **– The tree of the gods viz. **कल्पतरु **which grants all our desires when we sit under it. **दृग्विषयः अमूः **– I have seen you. **कामात्रा **– what is the value of this field i.e. it is very insignificant. **पुरुषप्रमाणे गर्ते सवृत्ते **— when the pit had been dug man-deep i. e. 5-6 feet. **चन्द्रकान्तशिला**–the moonstone, **बलिहोमपूजादिकं विना **– without performing, Puja, Bali, (offerings of food), Homa etc. **विधानम्**–ceremony. **शेमुषीविधुरः **—
devoid of understanding **(शेमुषी)**. i. e. **ग्राह्यवचनम् **– sound advice. **नान्तरायलेशः **— not the slightest impediment. **आगामिनः अर्थाः **– future objects. **अनर्थकार्ये प्रतिघातनार्थम् **–forwarding off from evil deeds.

** (34)** **अन्योक्ति **– is a figure of speech, where apparently some one is addressed, but it has reference to some other object. Thus, in these lines, the lion is addressed but the lines have got quite a different meaning and application. **असहायः **– without any help from others. **अपरिच्छदः **— without any covering. Stanz 2. The lion cares little if men call him. **मृगेन्द्र **(which is a respectable term, the Indra of elephants) or **मृगारि** (lit the enemy of beasts, which is a contemptuous term); he is indifferent to all such terms. **व्रीडा **– shame. **क्रीडादलितदन्तिनः **– who crushes elephants very easily. **क्षेत्रम् **– field, a plot of ground. **नरैः तृणमयैः अपि — **even with sham forms of men made of hay, (the deer can be scared away).**मृगैः नष्टम** &c.– After hearing the neighing of horses, deer disappeared, hores fled away, the bears turn round in rage but the lion was steady as before. **अराजलक्ष्मणि **– not having any sighns of royalty. **सर्वोत्कट**—all powerful. **राजा इति गिरः परिणमति**–All men call him “a king” though etc.- (lit. words fall down, “that he is a king”. **यथा तथा**–In as much as **बृंहितम्**—Roaring of an elephant. **गजेन्द्रपलकवलनः **– to whom the flesh of elephants is a month ful. **शङ्कातङ्काय कल्पते**–is able to create fear, auguish **(आतङ्का)** in their minds **यूथनाथः **— the leader of the herd (of elephants). **आखुबिलम् **– the under ground nest of rats **पाषाणशकलाकुलम् **– full of pieces of stone. **उच्छायवती **– big, **दशन **– Tusk, tooth **दीर्घदीर्घः **— very long. **कराः **— Trunk (of the elephant). **अम्बरैः स्पर्धते **– does not compete with you in rich dress. **वेधसा**–by the creater. **अजेयं तेजोबीजम् **– invincible spirit. **तादृकृतादृशम्** etc.–He regards only appropriate beasts as his prey.

** (35)** **वैतालिकः **– A bard. In the Sloka, the last line says “Victory to the king Bidaha” and the 1st, 3 line describe the different types of men who praise him. **सन्तुष्टचित्तैः विप्रैः **- Brahmins, having the cravings of their heart gratified **प्रमुदितहृदयैः लब्धकामैः बन्दिभिः **— Bards delighted at having their desires satisfied. **वश्यताम् आश्रयद्भि दिगवनिपतिभिः **– princes from all directions seeking his support. **वृत्तिः **-avocation. **निवोध्यति **– urges to fight **वचोभिः कापुरुषात् कौत्स्यं विमोचयति **— causes by his speech, the wicked to abandon their crooked ways. **(कुत्सस्य भावः – कौत्स्यम्). विपक्षवचनम्**–accounts of his enemy. **कृपणतां न याति**—is not degraded. **अर्थैः**–with money. **अङ्कुरितं यशः पल्लवयामि **– Note the methphor. I spread forth their budding glory. **सामर्षः (आमर्षेण सहित) **– full of anger. **सुवर्णायतनम् **– a golden house. **नतथम् **– falsehood. **कीर्तिगाथा **– songs of his praise **चारपुरुष **–spies. **तथ्यावाग्–तथ्यवाग् यस्यसः**—If what you say turns ont to be true etc. **धातुः प्रपञ्चे**—In the world of the creator. **राज्यधुरं सचिवे सन्निवेश्य**–having entrusted the administration to his minister.

** (36) सुभटवेषधारी **— refers to **विक्रम **– wearing the dress of a warrior **अनन्यसमसहायः **– whose daring is not equalled by others. **दौवारिकाः **– doorkeeper. **प्रत्यहम् उत्पद्यमानम् **– created a new every day. **वितरणम् **– giving over. (in charity). **पुरुषाधीने–उदासितव्यम् – **A man should not despair of achieving things which (another) man can accomplish. **जिज्ञासुः **– desiderative from **ज्ञा**. **निभृतक्रमेण तेन (वडाहेन) अनुपलक्षितः **– unnoticed by Biduha who was going with silent footsteps (**निभृत** silent **क्रम **– footsteps **पदास्फालन **— beating of feet. -**फेत्कार**—howls. **नरकपालैः**–( skulls of men ), **भारचिताङ्गारैश्च** (**भारचिता **– funeral pyre, **अङ्गार **– burning charcoal) **चित्रितम्**–qualifies **श्मशान.** **भैरवपुरुषैः **— fierce men. **नरचर्मरज्जु **– ropes made from human skin. **प्रवलेन अनिलेन सतप्तं तैलं. तेन पूर्ण **— **प्रवनानल** ect–filled with oil heated by a strong fire. **कटाह **– frying pan compare **कढई** in Marathi. **तैलसुसिद्धानि **– well cooked in oil. **चामुण्डा **– a terrific form of the goddess. **दुर्गा वन्दान्यता सम्भावितस्य **– well known for charity. **अर्थिजन **– beggars. **अगार **– house.

** (37) प्राणपरितर्ने **– lit. exchange of life. At the cost of his life. **एके न एव प्राणपरित्या** etc.—She does not bless him if he ventures his life once only i. e. Badaha had to kill himself every day; as will be seen later on, through Vikrama's intervention with the goddess, this sacrifice of life everyday was stopped. **अग्रिमनिशायाम्**–earlier part of the night. **सचिवसामन्तभृत्यपरिवारितः **– surrounded by ministers and attendants. **प्रदोष **– twilight. **निःपरिजनः **– without any attendans **झम्पकम् अकरोत् **– jumped (into the pan) **आद्रमांसयोगात्–शब्देन**– A peculior sound **(तटकटा)** being produced by the contact of Vikram’s wet body with the boiling oil. **बडाहभ्रमेण **– Thinking that he was **बडाह. लब्धाष्टसिद्धिः **– One who has attained the eight superhuman powers. **वडाहे कृपार्थम् **– for haviny pity for **बडाह. यथार्थवचनम्**–whose words has proved out to be true. **आकाशवाच् – **A speech from the sky i. e. a speech from the gods. **अनिर्धारितवाक् **– of which he did not understand the meaning. **प्रकरण बलेन **– by reference to the context. **मरणायासनिरपेक्षा सिद्धिः **– he could have his golden house now without killing himself **अर्थ पुनरुक्तं चकार**–doubly assured him. **विक्रम केसरी**–**विक्रमः केसरी इन – **Lion like Vikrama construe **यत् यया दानवीरे अपिकल्पवल्लीव कल्पयते **– by which are served philanthropists like a creeper fulfilling all desires. **कल्पवल्ली **– cf. **कल्पतरु**. which is more common. A desire granting creeper.

** (38)** **अम्मोधेः तीरसंश्रयः **– While standing on the shores of the ocean **तन्मनस्कतया अभिष्ठ्यमानः **– praised fervently by him. **अस्पष्टमूर्तिधरम् **– With an indistinct from. **वन्हिपिण्डोपमम् **– like & ball of fire. **प्रसादीकृतं विशेषम् **– special favour. **आताम्रोज्वल –ह्रस्ववपुषम्** -possessing a red, shining and short figure. **इषदापिङ्गलनयनम् – **with stightly tawny eyes. **कृतप्रणिपातस्तवादिकञ्च **– who had performed salutes adoration etc. **वियत् **– sky. **स्वधिष्णम् **– one's own **अमलमणिरत्नसनाथकण्ठतया **– with the pure jewel adorning his neck **अवनिभारवतरणाय **– to reduce the burden of this earth i. e. to free it from sinful persons.**भगवन्तम् **— refers to Shri-krishna. **विश्रब्धाः पश्यत **– look at him without any fear. **निवेशन **– house **रत्नप्रवर **– excellent_jewel. **स्रवति **– produces. **उपसर्ग**–pestilence. **व्याल** a wild beast. **दुर्भिक्ष्य **– famine. **लिप्सा **– desiderative from **लभ्**–desire to obtain. **गोत्रभेदभयात् **– out of fear of civil dissentions **शुचि **– a holy or pure man. **साश्वं – (अश्वेनसहितम्)**–along with the horse. **आस्येन आदाय **— taking it, in his month. **सुकुमारसञ्ज्ञाय **— to his son, by name Sukmuara. **कर्णाकर्ण्यकथयत् **—spread rumours (lit. whispered into other's ears). **प्रसेनाश्वपदवीं** **अनुससार **— followed up the footprints of Prasena's horse. **अखिलजनपदमध्ये सिंहपददर्शनकृतपरिशुद्धिः **—He was seen to be faultless by all men when they saw the track of lion's feet. i.e. from the track of lion's feet, all men came to know, that Krisha was not to blame in this affair, as the deed was committed by the lion. **तद्रत्नगौरवात् **– owing to the importance of the jewel. **धात्री**—Nurse. **सुकुमारकम् उल्लापयन्त्याः **- reconciling the child (qualifies **धात्री**). **लब्धस्यमन्तकोदन्तः **— who had learnt all the history of the jewel. **तदर्तनादश्रवणानन्तरम् **– After hearing her cry for help. **तरक्षु **— hyena; here stands for bear. **तन्निष्कान्तिम् उदीक्षमाणाः **– waiting for lion to come out. **मधुरिपु **— Krishna; Madhu was a demon killed by him. **उपरतक्रियाकलापम् **– funeral ceremonies. **अतिश्रद्धा** etc.– **अभूत् **– krisha was nourished and increased in vigour owing to the food water etc, offered devoutly and to proper persons. (This refers to the funeral oblaitions offered by his relatives.) **अतिगुरुपुरुषभिद्यमानस्य **— struck by a very powerful man. **अतिनिष्टुरप्रहांरपीडिताखिलावयवस्य **— whose whole body was paining owing to the very sharp blows. **निराहरतया **– being without any food.

** (39) अवनिगोचर **– living upon this earth. **तिर्यग्योन्यनुस्मृतिभिः **—Those who are born in lower grades of creation. (i. e. lower than that of man.) **अंशेन भवता भवितव्यम् **—you must be an incarnation of etc. **अखिलभारावतारम् आचचक्षे **– told him that he had come down upon this earth for lessening its burden. **गृह्यगमनार्घभूताङ्कन्यां **etc.–offered his daughter to him as a reward for his coming to his house. **अतिप्रणत**—too much humbled down **आत्मसंशोधनस्य**–to free himself from the guilt. **अतिपरिणत वयसः**–very old. **दिष्ट्या**—well done. **यथानुभूतम्**–all that he had experienced. **मिथ्याभिशस्तविशुद्धि **etc.—cleared himself from the false charge. **वयम् अपि अभ्युयपत्स्याम्**—we shall help you. **जतुगृह **etc.—a house made of lac, used by Duryodhana to burn the Pandavas. **विदितपरमार्थः**–Though he knew the real state of facts viz. that they were not really burnt. **कुल्ययरणाय**—all the (funeral) rites in accordance with the usages of tha family. **भगवते अहम्–अक्षान्तिमता**—enraged to see me offered to you.
-**अनुलङ्घ्यवरपादपम् **— lit. without ascending a tree i. e. without kicking it. **अलम्** **अत्यर्थ अमुना शोकप्रेरितवाक्यपरिकरेण**–Enough of all these sorrowful statements. **आवाभ्यां सामान्यं भविष्यति **— we are the joint owners of that **कृतोद्योगौ च एतौ उभौ उपलभ्य **— After learning that both (krishna and Balaram) were after him. **पार्ष्णि** back rear **पूरककर्मनिमित्तम् अचोदयत् **— urged him for backink him with help. **असुरवनितवैधव्यकारिणा **— who brings widowhood to the wives of demons i. e. who kills the demons. **प्रवरिपुचकाप्रतिहतचक्रेण **– whose chakra (a weapon ) is unobstructed even by the most powerful circle of enemies. **चक्रिन् **– one who bears a chakra **मनमुदितनयनावलोकितारिवलविशातन **— who destroys the forces of his enemy by a mere look of his eyes, expanded with the sense of his power. **सीर**—plough, the characterestic weapon of Balaram. **अतिगुरुवैरिवारणाकर्षणाविष्कतमहिमोरुसीरेण**–who uses his great plough for killing the elephants of his very powerful enemies. **अमर **— lit. one who neverdies i, e. i. the gods **शरणम् अभिलष्यताम् **— seek help. **अन्तायाम् अवस्थायां**–even at the last moment viz. of death. **पदातिः **– a pedestrian, one who walkson foot. **दृष्टदोषाः हयाः **–exhausted horses. **अलीकशपथैः**. false oaths. **गदाशिक्षाम् **— the knowledge of using the mace.

** (40)** **बलि **— wrinkles. **पलित **— white hair. **भ्रान्तम् **— we wandered. **ध्वाङ्क्षवत् **– like a crow. **साक्षेपभुकुटीकटाक्षकुटिलम् **— with the eyebrows knit contemptuously. **पातसज्ज **– ready for death. **अयत्नेन **– easily. **गोष्पद **— the quantity of water sufficient to fill the impression of a cow’s foot in the soil i. e. a very small puddle.

** (41)** **कृत्वावगतिभिः**–who had come to know. **सुवर्णध्यानपरः**–Always thinking as to how the gold might he used.**दीक्षाकवचं प्रविष्टौ** etc.–He who kills either Ksyatriyas or Vaisya, when they have taken the sacrificial Vow, incurs as much sin as if had killed a Bramhin. **मरक **– pestilence, epidemic disease. **उरगारिकेतनः** (**उरगाणां** serpents ) **अरिः केतनं यस्य** etc.– whose symbol was the eagle (enemy of serpents) i. e. Krishna. **गर्भस्य अनिष्कामतः **– without the embryo coming out i. e. the woman did not give birth to a child. **अतिगुणवति **– refers to Akrur. **कृतापराधतितिक्षाभवम् अभयं दत्त्वा **– after giving him assuarance that his past faults were for given. **स्वल्पम् एतन् कारणम् **— this is not a sufficient reason. **सुमहान् च अयं प्रभावः **— these results are very great. **यज्ञाद् अनन्तरं** etc.—He is performing sacrifice after sacrifice. **स्वल्पोपादानं च अस्य**–He has only meagre funds **प्रसङ्गागतपरिहासकथां कृत्वा **—after talking with him about usual and friendly affairs. **अन्यथा ब्रवीमि चेत् **– If I shall not tell the truth, **केवलाम्बरतिरोधानं **– which is merely hidden by the cloth, **अन्वेषणन्नक्षेमम् **– It is not desirable that they should search. **श्वः परश्वः वा **— tomorrow or day aftertomorrow **अतिकृच्छ्रेण **— with great difficulty. **अशेषोपर्भागेषु असङ्गिमानसः **– I could not turn wind to any pleasure or enjoyment. **आत्मनान चेदितम् **— I myself did not speak. **समुद्गक **– box or casket, **चक्रान्तरौ अवस्थितामिवमेने **— Krisha was put in a difficult position. **आत्मसंशोधनाय **– to free myself from all guilt. **अंशुमाली **– one surrounded by a garland of halo. **मिथ्याभिशास्ति **— false charge.

** (42)** **अलस **— Idle man. **उदयोगहेतुः उत्साहः **– Energy which is an incentive to industry. **प्राणिहेतुः **– duty of a man. **दुर्गतेभ्यः **– men in adversity; poormen. **दापयति **—causal of **दा** to give **निर्गति **– wretched condition. **जाठरेण अपि वह्निना **—(the fire sup posed to be in our stomachs exciting hunger.) Here it means, even for the sake of livelihood. **नात्मा चिकीर्षति **– does wish to do anything; does not take the trouble of speaking even. **निद्रासुखं **etc.–only pressing hunger can deprive him of the pleasures of his sleep i. e. will rouse to him to some activity. **तुन्दपरिमृजाः **– **तुन्द**–belly and **परिमृज् **– sluggish **वर्तुलीबभूवुः **– lit became round, gathered in large numbers. **सौकर्यमूला स्थितिः **– easy life. **अलसशाला **— home for the idle. **तन्नियोगिपुरुषैः **— men appointed there. **अक्षमबुद्धया **— knowing that they are incapable of exertion. **यथार्थालसान् परीक्षेमही **– we shall test, who are really idle. **करः **– mat. **केशेषुआकृष्यगृहीत्वा **– seizing them by their hair. **गतिः **– stay, something upon which to lean for support.**कारुणिकम् **– a kind hearted man.

** (43)** **चतुरङ्गबल **— A complete army having its 4 parts viz. elephants, chariots cavalry and Infantry. **क्रोडेकृ **– to clasp to the bosom. **चाण्डालशङ्कास्पदम् **— which gives occassion to suspect the deed of chandala. (in connection with its birth). **दशाविनिन्द्या **— The condition of life is to blame. **पुत्रगुणेननारी रत्नप्रसूः **— woman with a son has the credit of giving birth to a jewel. **भङ्गासहाः **– Intolerant of disobedience. **सौभाग्यमदगर्विताः **– elated with the pride of their beauty. **नीचानुरागिणीम् **– entertaining affection for the low born (viz, the child). **विज्ञानलोपकरः **– depriving a man of his power of thinking. **दशापरिणतिः **— fate. **दग्धारण्यभस्मना **— with the ashes burnt wood. **सपत्निखेता **– troubled by the rivals (i. e. cowives) **संव्यस्थरत्नाङ्गदे **– from which the jewelled armlets (**अङ्गद**) have been removed. **हारस्य त्यागेन हृता श्रीः ययौः तौ — **whose beauty has faded because of the neck lace being gone.**नूपुर **— anklets. **अङ्गानि एव निवेदयन्ति **— your very limbs say etc. **सुदति **— one with beautiful teeth. **सार्थनामा विशाखा **— my name is siginficant (because he had no **शाखा** i. e. line of ancestors). **तर्पयति **— offers libations. **मुक्तकण्ठं रुरोद **— wept bitterly. **मर्तुकामः **— **मर्तुं कामः यस्यसः**—desirous to die. **ज्ञातव्येषुच** etc– Translate: — In things to be ascertained according to their time and place, men can proceed to know it only with the knowledge of priority or posteriority. सेवक

** (44)** **सुखासिनम् **– Sitting at his ease. **शक्र **– Indra. **विदयाधरी **— a female demi god. **शृङ्गारचेष्टाभिः **– amorous gestures. **सदर्पकन्दर्पः **– proud cupid. **कमलदृशाकज्जलमलिन - कटाक्षैःकवलिन्तचेतः **— a mind overpowered by a lotuseyed woman with her dark (lit as lampblack) glances, **न वाञ्चति व्रीडाम् **– is not inclined to Shame. **प्रत्यभिज्ञान **– recognition. **प्रतिभया प्रगल्भः **– endowed with genius. **सेवकमुद्रया **– in the garb of an attendant. **प्रतीहार **– doorkeeper. **प्रभाव **– power. **राज्यसुभटचक्रम **– all the Warriors of the kingdom. **निजानुरक्त **— attached to hiin. **शृङ्खलाहस्त**—with chains in their hands. **आत्मानं परिचिनोत्येव **— he knows it himself. **अविलम्बितम् **– Instantly, without any delay. **शृङ्खलाहस्तद्वारा **– with the help of men who had chains in their hands **स्वस्वअतिरिक्तान् परस्परं कृतसन्धानान् अवगत्य **–everyone thought that save himself all had entered in to a conspiracy with him, as a matter of fact **(वस्तुतः)** none had so treated him **(अकृतसन्धानाः)** **एतावतां पुरुषतां** has attained to such eminence. **मन्त्री – **politician.**स्निग्धैः बान्धवैः प्राप्तः **– etc.–without affectionate relatives.**पित्रोः कथा द्योतिता **— Told **विशाखा**’s parentage to the king. **कृतिः**–work (drama) **मुद्रा– राक्षसं राजनीतिर्सवस्वम् **– the plot of this drama is wholly political and of this kind it is a master piece.

** (45) महेच्छ **— of noble desires. **न्यायेन उपार्जितं द्रव्यम्**—wealth acquired by honest means. **पुण्ययशसः पात्रम् **– fit for religious merit **(पुण्य)** and fame. **प्रभुसन्मानपात्रम् **—ever honoured by his master. In an address given to him. **धर्मार्थ **etc.–the four objects of human existence **(पुरुषार्थ)** are **धर्म, अर्थ, काम** and **मोक्ष**. **क्षयस्थिति वृद्धिपरामर्शसनाथैः **(qualifies **उपायैः**)—making full allowance for Expenses **(क्षय)**, maintainence and accumlation. **धर्माविरुद्धैः — **Not incompatible with religion. **यद्यपि अर्थः **etc.—There are 3 **पुरुषार्थ**s to be accomplished by man **धर्म, अर्थ **and **काम** ; though **अर्थ** is only one of them still, everyone talks about wealth. **कार्यभारस्य वोढा **(bearer) **असौ** etc.—he has only the burden of these actions but can not enjoy their fruits. **करोपातङ्गता** etc. – the ability to earn wealth is in the tip of his hands i. e. he can easily acquire wealth. **धनप्रयोजनं चिन्त्यं भवति **— the necessity of wealth should be kept in mind. **प्रस्थ **– a particular measure of capacity e.g. for measuring food materials etc. **प्रस्थमात्रं भुक्ते** etc—eats a particuler measure of food. **धनलाभफलभाजनं भवामि **— I shall enjoy the fruits of my acquired wealth. **स्रक् **—Garland. **इष्टापूर्त–इष्टं च पूर्तं च तयोः समाहारः **– Performance of charitable deeds. **तुलापुरुषादिदान **— gift of things weighed in & **तुला** (balance) against oneself. **विषयविरक्ति **– aversion to sensual pleasures. **व्रतोपवासादिकायक्लेशसाध्यम् पुण्यराशिम् **– morits, only to be attained by such mortifications of body as religions vows, fastings etc. **सर्वदर्पहर **– oldage, removing all pride etс. **अपचयम् **– decrease. **प्रभुशक्तयः **– exercise of authority over others. **देहश्रियः **– charms of my body. **तृष्णाविजयोत्सव **–To glorify our conquest over avarice. **वैभव **– here refers to wealth. **हरिश्चन्द्र स्पर्धया **– to emulate the fame of Harischandra who is very famous for **दानशूरता**. **अनशन विधिना **– by fasting. **आपरार्द्धम् **— Till it reached **परार्द्ध**, a figure higher than crores even. **के न अपर्यन्ति **is a question of A appeal. Who will not give i. e. All will give **उपद्वारम् उपागतेभ्यः**–coming to their houses. **अर्थान् प्रार्थकगेहम् प्रास्थापयत् **—He supplied money to supplicants at their houses.

** (46)** **लप्स्यमानधनावेशात् **– Imprudence due to acquired wealth. **कृतलब्धधनव्ययः **–Spending all the acquired wealth. **त्रिवर्गविषयविज्ञः** not knowing the 3 fold object of human life viz. **धर्म, अर्थ, काम. वृद्धोपदेशतः ज्ञानम् **– knowledge is acquired through the advice of the old. **प्रतिष्ठा **— honour social status. **सुलभम् **– cheap as opposed to **महर्घे **– dear buys cheap and sells dear. **मूल्यविभेद–**difference of value. **व्यवसायी **—active, industrious. **वृष्टिपाषाण – **hail. Just as hails in a shower are destroyed (i. e. melted) so with such women and such men. **भाव्यमानायां धनवृद्धौ **– when wealth can be muthplied in this way. **दशलक्षपरिशिष्टम् **— after keepingout seperately 10 lacs i. e. 90 lacs only. **धनोपर्जनायासमात्रपात्रं बभूव **– he merely suffered the troubles of acquiring wealth i e. did not enjoy it. **जातरमसः **— becoming rash. **धनं यस्य **– he who acquires wealth is only pained to squander it. **अन्येषां भोक्तॄणाम् **— those who enjoy wealth, acquired by another. **उदर्कम् **– consequence. **उत्सन्नम् अकरोत्**—squandered. **निःस्रव **— Without any springs. **निरुपाये गेहे **– In a house where no exertions are made. **उपाय **—means of acquisition. **पूर्वानुगत्या **— According to his past ways of life.

** (47) कलावान् **– the moon (**कला**–the digits of the moon) **ग्रावद्रावकर्मणि **– the act of the oozing away of the stone. It is supposed that the **चन्द्रकान्त** is a stone which oozes away **(द्राव) **under the influence of moon (and not the sun) **कर्मठः **— proficient in any work. **आलोकवन्तः **– possessing splendour. **भूतेशस्य परिग्रहः **—Acceptance by Shiva. **कपालानि **— skulls of men worn by Shiva. Only because both skulls and moon have been worn by him, these two things, can not be equal **विचेष्टितम् **– Movements **नक्षत्रराजस्य **– moon, lit. Prince of constellations. **परीक्षणस्य **etc. — It is crescent shaped when growing smaller and round when full. **शिरसाधार्यमाणः अपि –**Though borne on the forehead i. e. in an exalted place. **सोमः **— moon, also Name of Shiva. **कृशतां धत्ते **– is very thin, because the moon on Siva’s head is shown as having a crescent form.**कष्टः खलु **etc. – dependance on others is miserable indeed. **द्विजेन्द्रेण क्षान्त **— the moon has put up with the following disadvantages etc. **सुरतटिनी** etc.–out of desire to be near Ganges. (**सुरतटिनी**–Ganges, also borne on Siva's head near moon).**फणिफूत्कृतिः **– the hissing of serpents on Shiva's body. **इक्षणतीक्ष्णाशुशुक्षाणि **– the severe fire (**तीक्ष्ण**–severe **आशुशुक्षणि**–fire) from the eye (the 3rd eye of Siva which is supposed to burn everything when cast in anger upon it). **निजकरनिकरसमृद्ध्या **— with the full lustre of your rays. **पार्वण शशाङ्क **– full moon (on **पौर्णिमा**). **हतविधिः **— Wretched creator, so called because he does not keep a man in full prosperity for a long time. **व्यज्यमान कलङ्कः **— whose spot (what we see like deer on the moon) becomes more obvious. **सर्वश्लाघ्यं **— laudable because in his Waning condition, the spot was not visible. St. 8 when moon is wanings then the spot is not visible (He is not **मलिन**) and so he approaches the sun but when waxing, the spot becomes visible **(मलिनता)** and he is away from the sun. **मलिनात्मनः **— men of bad character. **सिंहिकातनयः **— Rahu, by whose attack, eclipses were supposed to be caused. **सागरसूनुः **– Moon, so cailed because, it was supposed to be taken out of ocean at the time of churning. **मृगं **— the deer mark on the moon is suppored to be a poor creature seeking moon's help. **शीतमयूख **— lit one with cool rays ie moon. **तत् सर्वं त्वया म्लनीकृतम् **— All those fine qualities, you have blackened because you, caused the **कैरव** lotuses (which bloom whenthe moon shines) to bloom forth after leaving away the a lotuses (which expand when sun shines.)

** (48)** **शास्त्रविद्य **— Learned in Shastras. **अर्कचन्द्रयोः पारगः **– whose intellect can perceive even the sun and the moon. **अत्याज्यं व्रतम् **— binding duty **दुर्गत व्याधितार्त**—poor, diseased and distressed. **कश्चित् **– Introduces a question **अकृतमद्यपान **—without drinking wine. **नीरुग **— free from disease. **पुरुषायुषम् **– a man’s life. **शास्त्रदृष्टिः **— ever abiding by the Shastras. **चिकित्सा **— diangosis. **ब्रह्मकीटः **– Great worm. **शिरोगः **– has bored into his skull. **शान्तं पापम् **— God for bid! **निश्चितज्ञानः **— one having full confidence. **सिद्धान्तदार्ढ्य **– firmness of conviction. **वर्णपदवाक्योपपचयमात्रकुशला **— Expert only at composing, letters,
syllables and sentences. **यथावत् –**To as much depth as was required **तत् सर्वसभ्यसाक्षिकमेव जातम् – **that has been witnessed by all the men in the assembly **सुरमण्डलीविरचितपुष्पवृष्टिसाक्षिकम्** attested by the shower of flowers from the gods. **धरा – **earth **रुग्भैषण्यबुद्धः —** knowing diseases and remedies; qualifies **भिषक् - सन्देहनिर्णायकः —** clearing up doubts; qualifies **मीमांसकः** viz **शबरस्वामी. जाताहङ्कारेण— **used in a good sense here. Justly proud.**पुलकित – **whose hair of the body stood erect in joy. **स्वायत्तसिद्धिः -** one who has attained **सिद्धि** the super human powers. **अदरिद्रीकृत्य —** freed from his poverty.

** (49)** **सात्त्विक —** Good man as opposed to **राजसिक** and **तामसिक . राजनियोगं कुर्वाणः — **executing the orders of the king **आजीव्यधनेन – **wealth sufficient for his maintenance. **आह्निकम् –** daily religions duties. **समयं निनाय – **He passed his time. गङ्गा अपि आह etc.— Of such a man, even Ganges would say “when will he come and purify me ” **अकृत्यं दूरतः त्यक्तम् –** I kept away from what ought not to have been done. **तत्त्वनिष्टैकभावेन – **devoting myself to the realization of the true self. **कूलात् – **from the bank. (touching the banks) **कल्लोल** ( surging wave ) **मालया —** with the waves dashing against the bank **शिशुमार – **porpoise. प्रवाहपतितोभयतटविटप- With the trees on both the banks felled down by the force of the stream. प्लाविताङ्गः—bathed in body. **विधिनियोगात् —** fortunately. **मुक्तिं गतः –** obtained eterral bliss **विरञ्चि -** the God Bramha. **कथासारे संसारे — **wordly life which lives only in tales.

** (50) नीतिः — **Moral rules or precepts. **किंशुकः – **a kind of tree. **किं कुर्यात् — **Lit what can he do? i. e. what can be get from. **समृद्ध – **prosperous. **उपजीविन् — **servants, dependants. **भक्ष्यम् – **begging. Abstract noun from **भिक्षा भारोपजीवनम् —** living by carrying burden, a porter's life. **विवेकमुक्त — **devoid of discrimination. **चण्डकोपः – चण्डः कोपः यस्य सः—** hot tempered. **आत्मीयः – **lit one's own i. e. friend or favourite. **जुह्वनं. होतारं ** etc.—a sacrificer **(होतृ)** who is offering oblations.

 **6.** Translate:—we must go to the palace and we must see the king's favourites, for though we may not get any advantage still evil consequences will be prevented. **अत्यासत्रा** **विनाशायः – **Note the use of the dative. "That which is for boded by a pertentous phenomenon is put in the dative case." "when too near they forebode a disaster." **मध्यभावेन सेव्यन्ते – **should be served, neither by keeping too far, nor too near but in an intermediate manner. **राजवह्निः - राजा च वह्निश्च –द्वन्द्व** compound. Similarly dissolve next compound, **सारासारपरिछेत्ता – **who is able to discriminate between good and bad. **पानासक्तः – **addicted to drinking. **न साधत्यर्थान्** – is not able to accomplish his ends. **वाडवाग्निः – **the submarine fire supposed to pervade through all the oceans. **पिबन्ननिशम् – **drinking water all the time.

 ** (51)** The passage is one single sentence; the various compounds are adjectives qualifying **भवनानि अनवरत अध्ययनध्वनिमुखराणि — **resounding with the noises produced by incessant study. **भस्मपुण्ड्रक — **A sectarial mark with ashes. **कपिलशिखा** etc. - **कपिला शिखा एव नालम् ।** **तद् येषान्ते ( जण्टिलाः ).** ascetics wearing tawny and stalk like locks of hair. This qualifies **बटुभिः कुशानुः —** fire. **केदारिका-**small meadows. **हरितायमान –** Green **कृष्णाजीनविकीर्णः** etc. – **पुरोडाशिय –** useful for offering as sacrifical oblation **श्यामाक — **a kind of grain—where the shymaka grains, for sacrifical oblations were being dried and spread upon the skins of black antelopes. **नीवारबलिः—**oblation of wild rice. **हरित** (green grass ), etc. – **समिन्धि** ( **समिध्–** sacrifical sticks for the sacred fire)—All these materials were required for everyday duties of the Rishis and were therefore brought by their disciples. **इन्धनगोमयपिण्ड्रक** etc =Full of Heaps of fuel and dung cakes. **आमिक्षीयक्षीर–**Milk fit for turning into curds. **विलिखित्** (imprinted) **अजिर** (court yard) **वितार्दिकानि** (a raised quadrangular seat)— where cow's hoofs were imprinted upon the raised seatin the courtyard. **कामण्डलव्यमूत्पिण्डमर्दन** etc. — where the ascetics were busy kneading the earth with water. **(कामण्डलव्य)**. **वैश्वदेवपिण्ड–** balls of rice offered to all deities. **हविः** (oblation ) **धूम धूसरित** ( Dusty, grey ) **अङ्गन** ( court yard ) **विटपि** ( trees ) **किसलय** (Tender shoots)—where the tender shoots of trees in the courtyard were rendered grey by the smoke of the oblation. **वत्सीय – **cowherd. **तर्णक — **calf. **लालित** – caressed. **ललत—** playing or sporting-where the calves were sportively moving, being caressed by the children of the cow herds. **शुक्रसारिका** etc. — the idea is this:— the bird **शुक** and **सारिका**, began to repeat what the Bramhins were saying; they, so to say began the study; and when they began to repeat, tne Bramhins stopped and in this way, they got rest during their studies. **चिरदृष्टानां बान्धवानां **etc.—This refers to Bana; going to the houses of relatives etc.

 ** (52)** The whole passage contains a single sentence with adjectival clauses qualifying **आश्रम. सदासन्निहित **etc.–All these qualify **काननैः —** Upto **काननैः उपगूढम्— **there is one clause The ashram was surrounded by forest. **सदासन्निहितकुसु **- where fruits and flowers were to be had at all time. **तालतिलक **etc.-Names of trees; where all these trees were in abundance. **एलालता** etc. — **एलालताभिः आकुलिताः** **या नारिकेलयः । तासा कलापः यस्मिन् तत् ( काननम् )—** where there were groups of cocoanut trees surrounded by the gar creepers. **लोललोध्र–पल्लवैः – **where the leaves of लोध्र. लवली and लवङ्ग were waving to and fro. **उल्लसित – पटलैः -** where there were heaps of bright mango blossom. **अलिकुल** etc. – **अलिकुलझङ्कारैः मुखराः** **सहकाराः यस्मिन् —**where the mango trees were resounding with the humming of bees. **उन्मद **etc.–where swarms of intoxicated cuckoos were making an uproar. **उत्फुल्ल **etc.– which were rendered dusky by the heaps of the pollen of full blown **केतकी ** flowers. **पूगीलता** etc.-where sylvan deities were rocking themselves upon the swings of qua **पूगीलता** (creepers). **तारकावर्षमिव** etc.–where there were incessant **(अनवरतम्)** showers of very white flowers as they were shaken by the winds. The author compares these to the showers of shooting stars **(तारकावर्षम्)** which indicate the disappearance of unrighteousness **(अधर्मविनाशपिशुनम्)** The principal clause is **दण्डकारण्यस्थलीभिः उपशोभितप्रान्तम् –** whose outskirts were adorned by plots of a **दण्डकारण्य **forest i. e. which ( hermitage) was surrounded by etc.—the remaining words qualify **दण्डकारण्यस्थलीभिः . अचकित** etc. –** **where the cows **(शबला)** and hundreds of black antelopes were moving without any fear **(अचकित).** **मारीच - लताभिः —** where the **(वीरुदलता)**. were growing after they had been pruned by the false deer **(मारीचमायामृग).** **अशून्योपकण्ठम् – **Those neighbourhood was full of **उत्कण्ठि– ध्वानम्– **where the noise made by the filling of water jars was heard by swarms of peacocks with their necks uplifted taking it for the uproar of clouds **अनवरत** etc. — **चित्रभानुभि –** The firegods pleased with the inces- sant oblations of ghee. **उद्धूयमान** etc.–who had built a stair- case for going to heaven in the form **(छलना)** of the rising line of smoke. The poet methaphorically speaks of the lines of smoke as if it was a staircase to carry the sages to heaven **तपोधन** etc.–whose darkness had disappeared (be- cause of the sunshine) as it were, on account of the nearness of the hermits. **तरङ्गपरम्परा** etc. – **विगाह्यमानाभिरिव –** The disc of the sun was reflected in the waves of the water of the well and hence these several discs are compared by the author to the **सप्तर्षि** (the constellation of seven stars who had come there to see the sages. **अनिलावनमित – लताभिः –** The bending of the creepers due to winds, the auther fancies to be a mark of reverence for the hermits the same idea is repeated in some more clauses. **उटजाजिर — श्यामाकम् —** in whose courtyard the **श्यामाक **grain was spread for drying. The passage contains many expressions parallel to those in lesson **51. अनवरत–कुलम्–**where the parrots were uttering the **वषट्कारः**(an exclamation used in offering the oblations to deities) which they had picked up, having been heard by them manytimes. **एणीजिह्वा एवं पल्लवम् । तेन उपलिह्यमानं मुनिबालकं यस्मिन् । एणी –** A female black autelope; her tongue being very delicate is compared to a leaf **उपलभग्न–तलम्** where the surface of the stone slabs was rendered greasy by the oil of cocoanuts broken on the stones. **इतस्ततः – परिहारम् – परिहार – **common land round & village or town. The dining place of the sages is compared to a town and the line of scattered ashes is said to be its **परिहार. परिचित – तापसम् – परिचित–** ( familiar ) **शाखामृगैः** ( monkeys ) **निकास्यमाना । प्रवेश्यमानाः जरदन्धतापसाः यस्मिन् ।** **इभ–पतितैः –** which had fallen down after beng half eaten by the cubs of elephants these lotus stalks are compared to Saraswati's bracelets. **विषाण–मूलम्–**where various tubers and roots were being dug out by the black. antelopes with their pointed horns. **पुष्करपुर –** a cup made of lotuses. **विटपालवालकम् —** The basin round a creeper for holding water. **वनवराह – शालृकम्– **the roots of the water lily stuck into the teeth of the wild boar. **पक्षपुटव–शनम् —** where the peacocks were kindling the sacrifical fire by the flapping of their wings. **पुरोडाश –**sacrifical oblation **अविच्छिन्न** etc.— **अविच्छिनैः आज्यधारैः आहुतस्यहुतभुजः** ( fire ) **झङ्कारैः** (noise ) **मुखरितम् \। उपमृज्य** etc. – **उपमृज्यमानम् उटजस्य अभ्यन्तरं यत्र ।—** Where the interior of the hut was being cleaned. **गवेधुकम् –** a kind of grass eaten by cattle **परिव्राजकम् –** Ascetic. **अदृष्टपूर्वं कलिकालस्य –** Which had not seen the कलि i e bad times. **अब्जयोनि–** the creator **ब्रह्मदेव**. From aut fi etc. the epithets apply to the Ashram and the thing compared. Hence there are punsupon the words and we have to find out the double meanings. **प्रकटितवराह** etc.—In the case of Vishnu, **नरहरि** and **वराह** are the two incarnations; in the case of Ashram, it had within itself, men, monkeys, boars etc. **साख्य – **a system of philosophy whose great master was **कपिल आनन्दित–कुलम् –** In the case of **उदयन**, **वत्स**s were his subjects; in the case of **आश्रम, वत्स **young children,**प्रत्यासन्नजलप्रप्रातम् – **In the case of Ashram, **(1)**.where water falls were in the vicinity **(2)** in the case of , where rainfall was imminent. **प्रारब्धाग्निकार्यम् –** In the case of **आश्रम (1)** where the worship of fire was began **(2)** in the case of Arjun, preparations for setting the forest on fire were begun. In some of the following epithets, the auther shows **विरोध** , punning upon the double meaning of the words. **मातङ्ग **means **(1)** a low caste man or elephants; here it means elephants. **उल्लसित **etc – **धूमकेतु — **means a comet which forebodes calamities **(उपद्रव)**; but the Ashram was free **(प्रशान्त); धूमकेतु** here means fire. **द्विजपति —** epithet of moon or Bramhan. The contradiction is removed if we take it to mean Bramhan.

 **(53) सः — **refers to Arjun. **मेरुमहीभृतः – **Of the Himalaya. Arjuna's coming to the Himalaya mountains is ascribed to 3 possible causes the remaining slokas describe the Himalayas, being epithets, (in the accusitive case) qualifying **हिमाचलम् ।**. **St. 2.** The mountain was lighted on one side by the sun and on the other there was continuous nightly darkness and hence it is compared to **शिव** who appears white (in froat) owing to the splendour of his laughter **(हसित)** while he appears dark behind, owing to his being surrounded by the skin of the elephant **(गजचर्मणा अनुगतम्)**. **St. 3.** **कृतनिकेतम् –** was made a place of residence by **अन्दृष्टपरस्परैः – अदृष्टाः परस्परे ( अन्योन्ये ) यैः ते । —** Who could not see each other construe, **शम्भुना जगतां विभुतां प्रथयितुं प्रतिनिधिम् अभिनिर्मितम् इव ।** who was as it were created by Siva, as a representative to demonstrate his mastery of the worlds. **St. 4.** The peaks of the Himalayas, **(सानु)** adorned **(कनकराजिविराजित)** with lines of gold **(मुजगराजसित)** white as the Lord of serpents and almost touching the skies **(नभ श्रिता)** cast into back ground **(लघयता)** the group of autumnal clouds **(शरदम्बुदसंहति),** elevated on mountain peaks **(निचयेन समुदितम्)** and accompained by flashes of lightning **( तडिद्वतीम्).** **St. 5. पुर इव भुवः दधतम्** bearing on it plots of ground resembling towns; the other epithets qualify **भुवः मणिमयूख – मणि मयूखचया अंशुकानीव । तैः भासुराः। सुरवधु** etc. —** सुरवधुभिः परिभुक्ता लतागृहा इव यासु । उच्चशिला** etc.—** उच्चानि शिलान्तराणि गोपुराणी** **यासु ।** where** **there** **were caverns in high peaks resembling the gateways **St. 6.** **अम्बुदैः उदितपक्षम् इव-** whose wings were as it were, represented by the clouds; the poet takes the clouds to be the wings of the Himalayas. The remaining words are adjectives of **अम्बुदैः अचिरद्युति** (lightning) **तेजसा विरहितैः -**free from the flashes of lightening. **आरतनिस्वनैः –** whose roaring was stopped. **पुथु –विलम्बिभिः** Hanging upon the **(पुथुनितम्ब)** broad Hanks of the mountain. **St. 7. तटैः नदीः दधतम् –** bearing the rivers on its banks **असमैः —** unequalled, incomparable. **विविधकामहिताः –** fit for a number of purposes. **जवनाः –** rapid. **St. 8**. The idea is : —There were jewels in Where there were the golden walls of the peaks, and the mountain looked as if the sun, were shining there with his evening rays **(विहितमयूरव मिव). नवविनिद्र** etc. – **नवानि विनिद्राणि ( विकसितानि) यानि जपाकुसु मानि तेषां त्विष इव त्विषो येषां ते ।. महाश्मनां निकरेण –** by the collection of jewels. **विहित** etc. – **विहिताः सान्ध्या मयूरवा यस्मिन् । तमिव स्थितम् ।. St. 9. पृथु कदंवकदम्बकराजितम् —** adorned with large flowers of the **कदम्ब** tree. **ग्रथितमाल –** which had formed a garland i e which was arranged in a circle. **लघुतुषार** etc — **लघुतुषारं (अल्पशीकरं) यत् तुषारजलं (हिमोदकं) श्चयोतति ( वर्षति ) तं धृतसदान** etc. — which contained intoxicated **( सदान)** and hand. some **(सदानन)** elephants. **St. 10.** The poet says, it does not bear certain things destitute of certain appendages i. e. it bears all these things together with their appendages. Thus, it does not bear peaks without jewels **(रहितचयान्)** i. e. it bears jewelled peaks. **दरिभुवः –** caverns, **(गुहाप्रदे । शान्). विपुलिनाम्बुरुहा सरिद्वधूः — सरितः वध्वः इव )** womenlike rivers without banks and lotuses **महीरुहः – **Trees **अमरलोकवधूजघनै; व्यथितसिन्धुम्– **where the rivers **(सिन्धु)** were agitated **(व्यथित)** by the waists of the wives of the gods (when they bathed) **अनीरशनैः – **with the girdle. **(अ+नीxरशना** . Two negatives.) **धनैः–** heavy. **दयितरम्थलताबकुलैः –** To whom the charming creepers **(रम्यलता)** and the stamens ( of flowers ) were very dear. **St. 12. शिखरैः अम्बुचयां चयम् उपविभ्रतम् –** bearing on its peaks a collection of clouds **ससुरचापम्– **accompanied by the rainbow. **ध्वनितसूचितम् —** ascertained by its noise. **St. 13. शुचि मानसम् –**The pure manas-lake. **शिवं दधतम्** –Shiva was also staying there. **अगात्म-सकलहम् —** who had quarreled with the angry **(कृतेर्षा) पार्वती** (lit the daughter of the mountain- **अगात्मजा**). **St 14.** The mountain lighting up ( lit burning **(ज्वलयता)** the planets **(ग्रह)** and the balloons **(विमान)** at the end of the day **(दिवम् अभितः) **, by the glare **(कृशातु)** of its phosphorescent herbs **( ज्वलयता, औषधिजेन ),** reminded **(अनुस्मरयन्तं )** every night **( अनुक्षपम् )** the devotees of Siva **( उभापतिसेविनः )** about the burning of the **3** cities ( **त्रिपुरदाह** of the demon ). **St. 15.** **विततशीकरराशिभिः –** with volumes of spray rising. **उपलरोधविवर्तिभि – **whirling on account of the obstruc tion offered by rocks **धृतसितव्यजनाम् इव —** the river Ganges seemed as if wearing a white garment owing to the water etc. **उन्नतसानुसमुद्धताम् –** flowing across the high peaks **धनाधिपतेः अनुचरेण – **the servaut of **कुबेर ( धनाधिपति )** i.e. **यक्ष.** **नग - **mountain **मुखरता – ( वाचालत्त्वम् ) —** garrulousness **अवसरे – श्रोतुः आकाङ्क्षासमये – **lit. at the proper time i. e. when the hearer is anxious to know. Mallinatha explains : – **आकाङ्क्षितम् अपृष्टोषि ब्रुयादिति भावः**

 ** (54) लोककर्मणि —** ways of the world. **लोके फले सादृश्यवान् – **In this world, he gets the same fruit ( of his labours ) that & learned man gets **शरावपरिमिता - शराव** is & measure of corn. He was given one Sharawa of Barley. (lit; barley measured by **शराज**). **भक्ष्यत्वेन –** By way of food. **यः प्रत्युद्धारे समर्थः भवति – **who will be able to deliver us from him ( i. e. king ). **परामर्शेनः** etc. — with the consideration of his family **प्रस्रवगृह –** urinal. **पानीयपरिचारिका –** A maid servant whose duty it was to bring water. **चेटी–** A fomale servant **परस्परविरोधिनी
- **contradictory. **लब्धावधिः -** Having got sometime. ( to think upon ) **सुबुद्धिपरामर्शपरिच्छेद्यम् एतत् –** This ( riddle ) can be solved only by the judgement of a clever man. **विधि निदेशतः —**out of misfortune. **विना देशकालानुसारिणा प्रकरणज्ञानेन – **without the knowledge of the context referring to time and place. **अवसर**-occassion. **तर्हि** **पूर्व** etc. — **हासनिमित्तत्वम् -** the laugher was not caused by anything seen before **हासस्य** **वस्तुविकृतिजन्मत्वदर्शनात् –** It was due to the sight of a production of change of matter. **विकृत**, **विकृतिः** — change. **महापरिणामम् –** having a large expanse. **अहो वैकृत्यं** faurg: gia-0 ! the mutability of things in the productions of the creator. itaa-decided. (**55**) Lesson, **इदं निर्द्धारयितुम् अलं भवति —** will be able to solve this (riddle). **तर्कः – **Reasoning **राजचर्या –** Performance of the kings service. **दुर्नीतिः –** wicked policy. **यमपत्तनयात्रायाः – अपेक्षते — **He only awaits the path of the pilgrimage to the city of Yama; i. e. he is sure to perish when he covets the friendship of those whom he has offended. **कथं वा ममापि** etc.–**अस्मिन् —** or again, how can my mind have confidence in this evil minded king **दृष्टा वैरक्रिया यस्य **etc.-He, who places confidence in another who has shown his deadly enmity to himself, perishes by death. **जिघ्रति -** from **घ्रा** to smell. **परा पर्यन्तघातिनी – **extremely destructive **सन्दिग्धचित्तः अस्मि –** I am in suspense **पश्यतोमम -** before my very eyes. Such a construction gives great emphasis, ef **नन्दाः पशाव इव हता पश्यतो राक्षसस्य ।**. Sloka **4**. He does not care for the loss of his wealth but wants to revenge himself for the death of wives and children. : **न वै माशां-**men like me are not dejected by it. **लक्ष्मीचञ्चलताभृता भृता एव –**wealth is always unstable. **ते **-Those well known. **सदसि प्रगल्मवचसः – **bold in learned assemblies. **सानुरागाः - **affec tionate.: **न मे चेतः मुञ्चन्ति –**These, I can not forget; (as I can the loss of wealth). **तेन अधमपुरुषपदवीनः –** so that I should not be regarded as a very base man. His idea was to punish the king through others; if he did it him- self, then people would regard him as meanminded when he was already honoured by the king. **पापानस्रस्यति–**Shrinks from sin. --who is afraid of incurring in- famy though of a sinful mind, construe:- **तस्य पातकात् अपि न ** **त्रासः। अपवादात् अपि न लज्जा । अयम् प्रज्ञावद्भिः अधमः उदाहृतः । अयं सर्वत्र निन्दास्पदम् । अपवादात् अपि न लज्ज-**who is not ashamed of a bad name. आराम ( gardens ) **दर्शन कौतुके न** — with & curiosity to see the gardens.**सागं वेदम् अधीत्य** -Having studied the Vedas together with their six Angas (or auxiliary parts or members. ) **विवाहार्थिता –** A desire to marry **विवाहभङ्गामर्षितः –** enraged at the obstruction to my marriage. **वृक्षायुर्वेद**-The **आयुर्वेद** ( science of medicine ) dealing with trees. **अधिगमः -** knowledge. **आभिचारिककर्मणि - **feats of a conjurer. **आभिचारिक** is an adjective from **अभिचार**-Employment of magical spells for malevolent purposes. **होम **- sacrifice. **अगारम् **- house **पुरोधसा सम्प्रधार्य** -having thought over the same with the help of the family priest. **पितृक्षयाहश्राद्ध **- Shraddha to (commemorate) the day of the death of one's father. **पात्रत्वेन उपनीतवान् **- in- vited him as the proper person ( to receive gifts). **श्यावनखदन्तः **- having dark brown teeth and nails **पात्रानर्ह – **unfit for receiving gifts. **पात्रासननिषण्ण–**seated upon the seat for the **पात्र. धमबाधां कुरुते -** destroys the religions efficacy. **दुर्दैवान्देशितेन-** Urged on by his evil fate **साधिक्षेपम् (अधिक्षेपन सहितम्) -** In- sultingly. **तथाविधानात् – **By that insulting conduct of the Nandas. **विचक्षणा परित्राता – विचक्षणा** was ( the maid servant ) saved. **वैरम् उद्धतम् – **took revenge for his enmity **अघ्नता** qualifies **शकटार – **who did not kill anybody but did it through others.

 **(56) विष्कम्भ** or **भकः –** An interlude between the acts of a drama, by which the reader is given a connected account of the plot. when only middling characters are introduced, it is **शुद्ध । **when by middling and inferior, it is called **सङ्कीर्ण **Construe :– **यथा इयं कविनां, कविता लोकत्तरे पुंसि नेवेश्यमाना, पुत्रीव हर्षं करोति, तया ब्रह्मविद्या न करोति, राजलक्ष्मीः न च करोति. ब्रह्मविद्या – **Knowledge of the supreme spirit. **साक्तम्–**Significantly, meaningly. **सकललोचनार्विदं मार्तण्डः —** Who is as it were, the sun to the lotus like eyes of all or who is to the eyes of all people what the sun is to the lotuses. **(सकलानां लोचनानि एव अरविन्दानि तेषां मार्तडः) पुरुषप्रकाण्डः —** an excellent man:- **प्रकाण्ड** at the end of a compound shows pre-eminency, excellence. ang- **कुलक्रमागतायाम् –** hereditary. **समीर-गुणेन -** With the strings **(गुण)** of the lute **(वल्लकी)** sounding **(क्रणात्)** sweetly **( कल)** by friction with the wind **(समीर) प्रतारितः अस्मि -** I have been deceived. **गगन तलालम्बिनोः – **Soaring high into the sky **सिद्धि -** the power of knowing the speech of the bees. ** वचनावबोध). विकस्वर – **opening, expanding. **चतुरालापपेशलता – **O, the charm of their skilful talk.** रुचिरनामधेयता** -the names of the two bees were sweet. **इन्दुमौलि — **Sive (lit, one with the moon upon his head)** दोर्दण्डमण्डलम् – **round arms i. e. powerful arm. **कैलासाधिकसाराम् **— **St. 2**. He wants to ask Siva where he can meet the equal of his arms on this earth: i. e. worthy field where he can show his bravery **कार्मुकम् – **bow **यस्य बाणानले** a-the etc.— Before the fire of its arrows the three cities were destroyed like moths. **तिस्रः पुरः - **were the **3** cities oelonging to a demon (who was hence called **त्रिपुरासुर** ) who was killed in a fight by Siva **प्राप्ताः पतङ्गताम् —** were reduced to the state of a moth i. e. Destroyed like moths by fire. garden of Indra. **निशाचर चक्रवर्तिन – **the emperor of the rovers ** **by night; this is an epithet of Siva. **अनर्चितचन्द्रचूडे – **while Siva is not yet worshipped. **लूनसकलप्रसूनं नन्दनवनम् –** how is the **नन्दनवन** deprived of all its flowers **(प्रसून). कुतुकित–मण्डनाय -** For adorning the balloons of the gods who are desirous to see the **स्वयंवर** etc. —** वृत्तान्तम् उपायनी करोमि —** I shall present this news ( **उपायन**-present ). **भ्रमारोपिताः** etc. - **सम्भवति -** the speech of these bees may possibly turn out to be due to an illusion **भ्रमेन आरोपिताः** ) **कुतो वा भ्रमरसम्भवना -** how can they be bees i.e. they can not bees; in fact, they were two bards. pleasing to the ear. **वन्दिनौ** — bards. **मकरन्द** - **धारिणौ** - producing as sweet sounds as the trickling of the juice from the flowers does. **घुणाक्षरन्यायः - घुणाक्षर -** An incision in woodor in the leaf of a book made by an insect and resembling a letter. Hence the maxim means any chance occurrence, due to an unexpected resemblance just as by chance the incision resembles a letter

 **(57)** The Pandavas had to spend one year incognito after **12** years in the forest; they had taken service under king Virata under various disguises; the kauravas got some scent of this; and to test this they mannaged to steal the cows of king Virata; this finally led to the discovery of the Pandavas. **अहीनवत्सा – **lit. not without calvesie with calves. **एकच्छत्रपृथिवीपतिः —** sole monarch. **वर्षवर्धनगोप्रदननिमित्तम् –** On the occassion of the gift of cows for the new year. **कृतमङ्गलमोदकाः — **who have prepared the auspici- ous sweetmeats **एषु ज्यैष्ठ्यम् अनुभविष्यामि —** I shall enjoy & posi- tion of pre-eminence among them (because) he was the most senior of all. ) **शुष्कशाखानिघट्टिततुण्डम् —** striking its beak against the dead boughs. **चन्द्रप्रभापाण्डुरण्योत्स्नावगुण्ठितः – **surrounded by a lustre as white (i. e. as mild) as that of the moon He means to say that as the sun was covered by the showers of dust, his dazzling lustre was dimmed and be- came as mild as that of the moon.**पक्कणम्** -A small hut. **दस्युकर्मप्रच्छन्नविक्रमः —** whose bravery is enveloped by an act of stealing. **निरीक्षणत्रस्तमुखैः — **Who were alarmed (lit whose faces) by looking (at the Kurus.) **आकुलाकुलम् —** **(अतिशयितम् आकुलम्)—**extremely agitated or disordered the repetition shows emphasis. **सदृशमेतत्** This is said ironically. **द्रोहिन —** perfidious, treacherous. **बद्धगोधाङ्गुलित्राः – गोधा** is & leathern fence round the left arm to prevent injury from the bow- string while **अङ्गुलित्र** is one to protect the thumb from the same **वर्मन्– **An armour. **कल्पितस्यन्दनस्थाः – **occupying well equipped chariots.** राज्ञो वैरं** etc.—Take revenge upon the cows for their emenity towards the king. **जन्मनक्षत्रक्रियाव्यापृतस्य – **engaged in looking to his horoscope. **पुष्याहावासाने— At the end **of the auspicious day i. e. when the ceremony would be over. **अतिपाति — **Running a rapid course. **St. 3** the king means to say that as long as he receives taxes from the people and is himself happy, the .cattle of his subjects should not be stolen; and he therefore contrasts his own comfortable position with that of the cows. **व्यथितविकीर्णबालवत्साः – **who are afflicted to see their young calves scatter- red from themselves. -by the apprehension **पीनांसः –**plump, fleshy caused by the clamour of chariots. **चलवलयः – **with the bracelets moving on it i. e. ornamented with the bracelet. **निर्लज्जः — **so called becaused it is not able to protect to the cows. **अवधूतम्मेक्षत्रियत्वम् **- my bravery has been washed off i. e. is useless. **एष समासः — **I shall tell you in short. **समासः **-Abridgement, conciseness.**कशापात—**lit the fallings of whips i. e. marks or traces left by whipping; the cows were whipped by the **कौरवा**s to drive them out. **St. 4**. He means to say. Originally the cows had one colour; later, there were the marks of whipping and the dust raised by the chariots setting upon these marks have made them of variegated colours. **रणशिरसि गवार्थे** etc – An attempt to fight for the cows would never be futile; even death would be glory to us; if we liberate the cows, we shall have done a pious deed. **कीचकानाम् — **Note that he uses plural for **कीचक –** as he had got respect for him. **उन्नीत-सन्तापाः – **One who is in distress. **परोक्षमपि पाण्डवानां स्निग्धः -** "Or Duryodhan might think that I am internally inclined to words the Pandavas **भगवान् दुयोधनस्य शीलज्ञ - भगवान् -** (i. e. **धर्मराज** who was staying with him under the disguise of a Bramhin ) is acquainted with **दुर्योधन**'s character.**अथित्वात्** **अपरिश्रान्तः** etc. - A man of action **(कार्यवान्) –** as he has to gain something **(अर्थत्वात्)** must make inquiries **( पृच्छत्येव)** indefatigueably **(अपरिश्रान्त). कृत्तपरिकराः –** who have girded up their loins i. e. who are quite ready. aft is the cloth worn round the loins. **रथाः सानूकर्षाः –**-well-equipped chariots. **श्रीर्न** etc.- A man who has wealth (lit wealth **श्रीः**) is never satisfied; it troubles those who are elated; while it frees those who are in difficulties. **एकोदकत्वम्** - Relationship (cf. **भाऊबन्दकी** in marathi ). **एकोदक -** Relatives connected by the offering of funeral libations of water to the same deceased ancester. etc.**यत्सत्यम् **- It is really we, who have done this mischief; he means to say that the Kauravas have at tacked Virata because they were staying with him and therefore, Relationship makes the mind of wise men even trembling. **निभृता भविष्यन्ति – **they will become humble; because he means to punish them. **St. 10.** The allusion to him in Virasa's speech greatly pleases (Virata does not know that **भगवान्** is **धर्मराज**) because, even in his absence, people know his for giveness **(क्षमा ज्ञायते मे)**; and therefore he says that all the sacrifices he had made upto that time have been well rewarded **(सर्व श्लाध्यम्). संश्रितानां निवासः —** staying as servants of another. **भग्नाः — **defeated. **धर्षितेन —**. refers to the **भट**. Though he is overcome, still he tells the news properly. **शङ्के तीर्णा प्रतिज्ञा इति ** etc.– I think he is proba- bly come to remind us that, we have fulfilled our Vow i e. we have passed **12** years in cogni to. **रणातिथिः - रणः एव अतिथिः** a guest in the form of a battlefield. **अमनोरथः –** is beyond expectation. **St. 15**. He means to say that the neither the fire of battle nor the Kauravas will spare his son because of his young age **अगणितगुणदोषः — **posessing innumerable faults and qualities. **बाल्यात् – **owing to
