the young age of **उत्तर. नपरिहरन्ते —**- will not spare. **न खलु **etc .— I am not pointing out these faults of war, out of disrespect to you. **सूतसमुदाचेण उपस्थितः **: etc.-I waited upon him with the eti- quette of a charioteer. **स्वचकोद्धतरेणुदुर्दिनम् -** making the day an unlucky one (**दुदिनं** for the enemy) owing to the dust raised by the chariot.**नेमिखैः** -by the mere noise of the wheel. **निमित्तम् **-an omen. **स्वस्थवाक्यम् -** Virata didnot like the humorous saying of **धर्मराज **explaining why the chariot was broken at the cemetry. **एषमाम् **etc.—He means to say, that, what the **भट** would speak, would not contradict him but would be as he had predicted. **St. 11** **नाग **- elephant. fa-double negative to give an emphatic affirmative. **स्यन्दनवरा — **the best chariots. **शरपरिकराः – **with arrows envelop. ing them. **स्रवतिधनुः** etc.-The bow sends down a terrific stream of arrows. the unexhaustibility of the quiver i. e. arrows were never wanting in it, it was always full of arrows. **खाण्डव —** was the name of a forest which Arjun had cleared off.: **धाराः **- showers of rain, (poured down to quench the fire burning the forest. qg etc.- what news about the enemy. **प्रवृत्ति **- News, intelligence. **द्वयोः वंशयोः —** Ambhimanu was descended from the Pandavas (Father's side) and Yadava's mothers side, **गीतः पितुः प्रत्ययात् –** who was well known **(गीतः)** because of the fame) of his father. viz. **अर्जुन. संसृष्टोपि **etc.–Though he is opposed to one who is fit to be his friend (because **अभिमन्यु** and **उत्तर **were of the same age) his equality of age will be able to protect him (from his enemy). **St. 27**. **योग्योपदेश** etc.— His chariot, as it were gives sound advice the first **3** lines describe what sort of advice it gives, by its own condition. **आलम्बितोः भ्रमति—** when checked (i. e. when the horses are checked to reduce its motion), it roams. **दिष्ट्याभवानूवर्धते –** you are to be congratu lated. **नन भगवत् :**etc.-No! No! This is all due to you. **अकालान्तरिता पूजा -** respect given at the proper time. **सविमर्शम् – **Expressing dis-satisfaction because being a warrior, **प्रतिस्पर्धितम्** he had to take a very mean character. f -I had to struggle i. e. I could not freely use it (be cause he was not accustomed to it for a long time.) **आ तत** **गुणे न -** with the bowstring stretched. **परिचयात्** etc — I re- gained my former skill owing to my past exercise i. e. he could handle the bow etc. skillfully after some time because he was formerly an expert. **जयगतः प्रहर्ष** delight owing to success. **समरमूर्धनि -** In the van of fight. **त्रिदण्डधारीन्** etc.- **त्रिदण्ड** are the **3** staves of a Sanyasi; **दण्ड **is the sceptre of the king; Arjun means to say that **धर्मराज** bears the marks of a Sanyasi and not of a king. **St. 36.** Virata means to say that the character of a man does not depend upon his appearance or family but upon the deeds that he does. **परिभूतपूर्वकम्** etc.-was insulted before but is respected now. **उर्जितं कर्म - **glorious deed. **अश्रद्धेयम् –** unexpected. **नुिहतेषु कीचकेषु** Kichaka being dead, there was no match for Abhimanyu **धर्षणम् **-defeat.** अवतारितः –**causal:-made to come down. **ईश्वरेण **cook. **महानसे — **kitchen **अपवार्य -** aside, to oneself. **परिष्वक्तः —** embraced, clasped.**येन सुव्यक्रकारिणा**-who has enjoyed **(निर्विष्टः)** the bliss of a son's ( embrace ) in a manifest manner (this refers to **भीम** ). **वृष्णि —** an ancester of the Yadavas **वयस्तुलयो** etc.—is of the same age as our son. **स्वविभवैः इष्टा** -are dear to us on account of their prosperity. **वक्तव्य परिहर्त्तव्यम् - **some part must be granted and some rejected. fa etc.- Long expected order. **शून्ये दृष्ट्वा -** Secing him alone. **स्वैरं तावत्** etc.-my son is ashamed to allow the tears to flow freely **(उब्दाष्पातां स्वैरंयातुम्)** in my presence (because of his defeat). **सङ्क्षेपात् **- briefly. **जतुगृह **- A house made of Lac where Duryo- dhan tried to burn down the Pandavas, Bhima means to say that his exertions in catching Abhimanyu were equal to those on that occassion. **भुजैकयन्त्रितः **-caught in his arms. **करेणुशोभाभिः अर्पितः-**decked with the ornaments of a female elephant. **दूषितो हस्तासारः ( हस्तेसारं यस्यसः )** My son whose bravery (lit essence) lies in his arm has been dishonoured -occurrence of what is desired. **St. 47**. **इहायं समुदाचारः —** This may be the etiquette here. He hints, that they lacked decorum. **ग्रहणं परिभूयते** - But my capture has put me out. **पितृवत् आक्रम्य** - addressing me like a father. **कुशली भवता संसष्टः —**They have been made all-right by you (ironical). **St. 50.** **हतेषुहि** etc.-only () look to the arrows in the bodies of dead men; and it would not be otherwise i. e. it would convince you about my bravery. **St. 51. सरथतुरग** etc.–Among the warriors and the elephants elated with the chariots and horses, there was not one that was not wounded by this expert in archery. **परिक्षतो भवेयम्—** I also would have been wounded.-
**शौण्डीर्य - **haughtiness pride. **पदाति -** etc.—an infantry soldier.**शेषाणां – दपि** etc.–You may pick up from the others i. e. his uncles whatever he chose. **प्रहरणम्– **weapon **सहजौ** -by themselves i. e. without the aid of bow etc. **पीनांस –**fat **निर्व्याजः – **Upright, honest. **अनुत्तरा –** we can not reply. **St. 57.** **असत्यं कर्म **- Jarasandha's killing was not according to strict rules of war. **कृष्णः अतदर्हतां नीतः -** Krishna was freed from the responsibility of such an act.**क्षेप –** abuse, insult. **रुष्यताभवतारमे – **I am delighted to see you annoyed. **St. 59.** **पादयोः समुदाचारः –**due honour. **बाहुभ्यां ** etc.–let Bhima carry away with his arms what he has brought with them. **St. 60.** **वाचानुवर्ती** etc – I am ashmed to speak when referring to the battle field. **St. 61.** **तूणी च अक्षयसायके –**Two quivers from which arrows could never be exausted. **St. 63. प्रकोष्टान्तरसङ्गूढम् – **Concealed behind the fore arm. **गाण्डीवज्याहतं किणम् – **the scar produceed by the bow string **नैव याति सवर्णताम् -**could not be of the same colour as the rest of the body; i. e. the scar could not be removed though Arjun had not used the bow for **12** years. **St. 64.** This is a scar left by the movements **(व्यावर्तन)** of the bracelets **(परिहार्य)**; and the colour of the skin being their stopping here, it looks like a scar of **गोधा. (lit. one with four extremities). **St. 86.** The poet compares the king with his **4** sons to (**1**) **सुरगज** or **ऎरावत** . which had broen the pointed swords of the demons with its tusk, (**2**) politics **(नय)** with its expedients **(उपाय)** the adoption of which **(व्यक्तयोग)** was to be inferred by the success attained **(पणबन्ध) (3)** Hari, with his **4** arms **(दोर्भिः),** as long as the yoke **(युगदीघैः). तदीयैः अंशैः —** the **4** sons were portions af Hari himself.

 ** (60) समुपलब्ध — परितुष्टाः — **Pleased by obtaining the highest honours from the king. **आशिषा अनुगृहयमाणः –** blessed with their good wishes. **बहुबन्धुमध्यवर्ती —** in the company of many relatives. **सम्भ्रातपरिजन**–confused or bewildered attendants. **आसीनेषु गुरुषु –** after the elders had got a seat. **अर्चादिसत्कार भजमानः — **obtaining and other marks of respect. **अप्रत्यूहा–** unimpeded. **क्रातवी क्रिया —** Sacrifical duties. **सभ्यक्करणपरितोषितद्विजचक्रा – **where all the Bramhins were pleased by the proper performance, **अविकलमन्त्रभञ्जिहवींषि**–oblations offered with perfect Mantras. **प्रमाणम् **– the science of logic. **मीमांसायाम् अतिरसः —** exclusive attention to mimansa **मन्दी–रसः –** where the study of other sciences was neglected. **अभिनवसु भाषित सुधावर्षिणः –** Showering nectar in the form of fresh fine passages. **वैतानवन्दि –** sacrifical fire **कियन्– कृत्यम् –** what do we require. **रक्षति – भुजे —**while the emperor is protecting the earth with his arm. **कौसीद्य **– Indolence, sloth. **वेत्रासनम् —**cane–seat. **स्कन्धावारः –** Royal camp or residence. **र्पयवारयन् —** oncircled, surrounded. (**59**) **बलाहक**–cloud– **चातका–कारिणि–** causing** **affliction (of the minds) to the Chatakas. **कादब — **black** **swons. **ददुर – **frogs. **हंसपथिकर** etc. – **हंसा एव पथिकसार्थाः, तेषां ( निर्मलजलदानादिना ) सर्वातिथित्वम् –** who was the host of the travellers in the form of swans. **धौतासिनिमनभसि** –when the skies were as white as a sword. **सुनासीर –** ( **सुनासीर** – Indra ) **सौदात्मनी –** Lightning. **दामन्**–streak, line. **दामोदरनिद्रादुहि **– which broke the sleep of the lion **द्रुतवैदूर्यवर्णाणसि –** when seas **( अर्णंस् ),** had the colour of melted **(द्रुत) वैदूर्य. घूर्णमान – मघवति–घूर्णमाना ( भ्रमन्ती ) या मिहिका** ( fog ) **तद्वन् लघवः ( तुच्छाः) येमेघाः, तैः भोघः (निष्फलः)** **मघवान् ( इन्द्रः) यत्र**. **नीप**–The flower of kadamba tree ( said to blossom) in the rainy season. –Name of a tree fa–when the plantain trees **(कन्दल)** had no buds. **शेफालिका – निशे**when the nights were cooled down by the **शेफालिका** plant **यूथिका —** a kind of Jasmine. **भोदमान – दिशि** where all quarters were rendered beautiful by the full blown lotuses. **सप्तच्छद – समीरे–**whore the atmosphere was rendered tawny **(धूसरित)** by the pollendust **(धूलि)** of **सप्तच्छद** plants. **स्तवकित** full blossomed, **बन्धुर **– charming, **बन्धूक — **a kind of tree.**नीराजितवाजिनी–**when horses were adorned. **दर्पक्षीबौक्षके –** when the oxen were excited with pride. **जननि–रमसि— **When the dust of the flowers of **प्रियङ्गु** creepers was produced.

 ** (61) दुगूलपट्टप्रभवे –** prepared from silken **(दुगूल)** cloth **(पट्ट). गोरोचना –** A bright yellow pigment prepared from the bile of the cow. **तैला– मौलिः —** who had softened **(मसृणित)** his hair **(मौला)** (by applying) oil and the fruit of **आमलक**. ( a kind of tree).**कुसुमापीडः **– a garland of flowers. **एक शलाकारुचिः**, –whose eyes were shining, of account on the collyrium, painted with the pencil. **आसदी**–a raised seat in a hall or assembly. **तत्कालाप – पुस्तकम् –** the Puranik had removed the covering of string from the book; but the author fancies as if it was surrounded by the rays from his nails, resembling the fibres of lotus–stalk. **सनीड **– Near, proximate. **प्राभातिक **etc.–omitting the amount as indicated by the mark **(च्छेद)** showing what he had read in the morning. **गमकः **– kind of musical note. **गीत्या **– in verse. **मुख-खैः — **His voice is fancied to be as it were the tinkling of the anklets of **सरस्वती** who was near to his face (as he was a learned man) **श्रुति–गर्भम्––**containing verses pleasant to hear. **श्रीकण्ठ —** Name of a country.

 **(62) पितृव्य – **paternal uncle. In some of the following adjectival clauses, the adjectives have a double meaning one referring to Bana's cousins, and the other to the thing to which they are compared. **पितामहमुखपदमाः **– lotus like four months of the creator **(पितामह). सामप्रयोगललितमुखाः** **साम **means (**1**) the **साम ** Veda etc. (**2**) one of the **4 उपाय** surely **साम, दान, दण्ड, भेद गृहीतवाक्याः –** who had understood logic.

 **(63) दशन–मुखैदुना– **his moon like face (as it were) bathed the quarters in the lustre of its teeth. **दयितेन आयुषा** **व्ययुज्यत —** was deprived of his dear life. **आहित—ग्रहणः—**who had married a Bramhin girl. **मार्गणव्यवसेन**— addiction to war **कृकलास**— lizard, chamelion. **अवशाक्षहृदयम्—** who had no control upon his heart and senses. **वाहिनी—**river.

 ** ( 64 ) वलिना — महानागः–** Refers to on anecdote; Shri Harsha, liberated a king who was surrounded by an elephant. **शेषभोगिमण्डलस्य – कृता —** The king has shown mercy to the remaining **( शेष )** kings **(भोगिमण्डल). कृतपक्षाः –** have been made his allies. **एकप्रहार– तिना–** who strikes down his enemy **( अरान्तिः )** with one stroke. **तुषारशैलभुवः –** born from the snow mountain i. e. Himalayas.:–All these **एवमादयः — समारभाः —** arrangements look just like those of the **1st**. **युग **(period) viz. **सत्ययुग **where there was an ideal condition of the** **society **अयस्कान्तमणयः –** Beads of magnet **स्वभावसरसमृदूनी इतरेषाम् —** is contracted with **क्षुल्लकानां** **नीरसानष्टुराणि मनांसि —** the vir. tues of great men attract even the hardened and prosaic minds of of mean men; much more can they attract the uaturally tender and poetical minds of others. society **हितम् –** you have not spoken properly **कुतूहलम् अवकल्पयामि** – I shall disappoint your curiosity. **शक्याशक्य – शूनाः –** Devoid of judging what is possible and what is impossible.** समस्तव्यापि**– prevading **(व्यापि)** all the world. **( ब्रहमस्तम्भ).** **अधिगत – लघीयसी–** in significant, because it can utter only a few syllables. **क्वउपयोगं गभिष्यति —** where can it be better utilized. **परिणत– दिवसः –** the day is almost over **पश्चाल्लं भास्वरः –** shining on ccount of the braided, hair hanging behind him in the orm of its tawny rays. **भार्गवः रामः– परशुराम–**the lake of blood formed. **समन्त महा -हदे –** by the battle **(पञ्चक)** all round this is compared to the red lustre of the evening sky. – sun. **शोणम् –** Name of a river. **सन्ध्याम् उपासितुम्** to say their а prayers.

 **(65) कपोलकोमलः** –as delicate as the cheeks. **मुकुलित** was drawing to a close. **रविरथ – तमसि –** Darkness following upon sunset is compared to the Buffallo of Yama, running after the sun's chariot. **कुटीर**–hut. – **कलि–धूमे **–the smoke from the abodes of the priest reaching to the skies, removing as it were the sins of kali. **पुलिका –** A kind of cake **होमकपिला –** sacrificial, brown cow. **वैतानतनूनपात् **– sacrical fire. **विष्टर**–A seat.–**तालध्वनि**–sound produced by the beating of the fingers. **अन्तेवासिन्–** pupils. **गलत् – कारिणि –– गलत् ** (forgetting ) **ग्रन्थ दण्डकाः** ( Lines in the book ) **उद्भिरति यतः तस्मिन् वटर –** foolish **ज्योतिस् –** Light. **प्रदोष —** Night fall. **गोष्टी —** chitchat. **निमीलित –** **निद्राणाम्**—who could not get sleep though they had closed their eyes, **प्रतिपालयताम् **— expecting, waiting for.

 ** ( 66 ) यामिन्याः तुर्येयामे–** the **4th** part of the night **पश्चादङ्घि प्रसार्य – **stretching its hind feet **त्रिकनतिविततम् –** extended owing to the bending of the spine **(त्रिक). आभुनकण्ठः –** whose neck was bent or curved as he was reaching his chest **(उरसः)** with his mouth **( मुखम् ). सत्यं –** the mane **अनवरतचलन्प्रोथतुन्दः–** who was constantly moving his belly **(तुन्द)** and nostrils. **कुर्वन्–करिः **– Drawing his hips near to his mouth bending the hind quarters **कन्धरा –** Neck. **केसर – **mane. **कषाय –** tawny. **वुसकणम्–** particles of refuse or rubbish. **कोणम्–प्रान्तम् –** part **पक्ष्मन्–** eyelash

 ** ( 67 ) श्रीकण्ठजनपद –** A country, by narne **श्रीकण्ठ. पुण्यकृत् –** God. **वासवावासः –** heaven. **असङ्कीर्ण–स्थितिः – व्यवस्थः–** where all dealings were as in **कृतयुग **(the best epoch) there being no intermixture of castes. **स्थलकमल**–a land–growing lotus. **पोत्र**–ploughshare.**उल्लिख्यमानक्षेत्रः —**whose area was polished or painted with(**मृणाल—**lotus stalks) **पुण्ड्रे– निरन्तरः** wholly covered with **(सन्ततिः) **chains of the gardens **(कट) **of sugarcane**( पुण्डेक्षु ). क्षीरोद–सिक्ताभिः –** The sugarcanes being exceedingly sweet, the poet fancies as if they were watered by clouds who had drawn their water from the milky ocean **(क्षीरोद). सस्यकूट –** heap of corn. **खलधानधामभिः –** the inniates **(धामन्)** of the threshing floor **(खलधान)**. **जीरकजूटैः –** masses of cumin plants. **शालीय –** Rice field. **उर्वरावरीयोभिः –** the most excellent of all soils. **पाक** etc.–kinds of grain. **किमीरित **– variegated. **कोशी –** pod, legume. **गोधन –** a herd of cows. **आमयाशङ्क्या –** through fear of indigestion. **महिषपृष्टप्रतिष्टित **– seated upon the backs of buffaloos. **चटकः **– sparrow (following the cows to pick up the insect parasites).**अवटु** – Neck **शारीकृतोद्देशः **– whose regions were variegated with **शतमन्यु** An epithet of Indra. **प्रवेशः –** way. **काश्यपीपृष्टः –** surface of the ground. **विलोभमी गर्भः –** whose gardens **(उपनिगम)** were to be coveted. **कमभ** – а young camel **पीलु **– Name of a tree. **मातुलुङ्गीदल **– leaves of a kind of citrus tree. **आरुकः** – A medicinal plant. **तुङ्ग **– tall, lofty. **अर्जुन **– a kind of tree. **कूलकीलाल – **water of the ponds. **धराबन्ध **– boundary. **कृतसम्बाधः **– crowded with. **औरभ्रक **– flock of speep. – **वडवानां वृन्दैः –** by groups of horses, **प्रभञ्जन – **wind. **किशोर – **young one. **बाण – ** fire, **मुरज **– a kind of drum. **अवदात **– beautiful, **वृत्त **–round. **अभिगमनíयः — **served. **मृगमद –** musk **मगरोम –** a cloth prepared from the hide of the deer. **पादाः – **hillocks **द्विजोत्तम –** birds **पोष –** station of cowheards **इष्टका **– brick. **यूपदारु — **piece of wood for the sacrificial post. **टङ्कः — **stone cutter's chisel, **पटह**–drum **ईति – **calamities.

 **(68) स्थाण्वीश्वर – **Name of a country. **तत्र च** etc. —This refers to **श्रीकण्ठ आराम –**yarden. **चमरीबाल** — the hair on the tail of a female dear, **शिबिरसन्निवेशः **– A camp or intrenchment **वाहिनी –** river. **विपक्ष –** army. **भार्गण –** Begging. **मत्तकाशिनी –** A hand some woman. **लासक –** Dancer **वैदेहक –** merchants. **भान्तगगामिन्यः –** going upon elephants. **पद्मरागिण्यः **– women wearing rubies. **धवल – वदना –** whose face was very beautiful on account of their white teeth. **श्वसनः –** breath. **भुजङ्ग –** paramour. **कञ्चुकिन्यः – **females wearing dress. **कलत्र **–hips. In the next paragraph, the poeet fancies some things as quite sufficient for a particular purpose and the others are rejected as useless or redundant. **दामन् – **a garland **भारः – **is a mere burden. **अलक – **curls of hair. **श्रवणावतंसाः – **earornaments **आडम्बरा –** a mere external appendage. **जालिका **– a kind of cloth for covering head. **तन्त्री **– a musical instrument. **पटवासाः **– perfumed powder's **अङ्गरागः – **a scented costmetic. **श्रोणी —** hips. **चतुरस्त्रा –** charming. **पदाभरणकानि — **ornaments of the feet.
